1)  
The Four-Year Course to Overcome Hardships  
Jesus lived His entire life centered on God's heart, fulfilling God's will. He sought to reflect God's heart in His actions and aimed to fulfill His mission in the battle against the enemy, which included restoring the failures of historical ancestors. Knowing that this was God's hope, Jesus constantly reflected on His life to ensure He did not deviate from this standard, paving the way as a new pioneer.  
Unity of Heart and Heavenly Work  
From the very beginning, Jesus spoke with the determination to establish a world that the heavens and the spiritual realm desired. He acted with that heart. Such actions were protected by God, guarded by angels, and were the actions that humanity historically longed for; thus, those who violated them faced historical judgment and direct punishment from God, who comes forth with history.  
You must not forget that God has come to humanity throughout the ages with an indescribable earnest heart.  
Today, you stand before God's will, having been called as representatives of Abraham, Moses, or even Jesus' mission, centered on the ideology of unification since April 19, 1964, at Daegu Church. You must reflect God's historical heart and inherit the emotional tradition that God has established until now.  
God is watching me, the angelic world is watching me, millions of saints are watching me, and all the brothers of this era, whom God seeks, are watching me. Wherever I go, in alignment with God's heart, the entire spiritual realm moves with me.  
If you move forward with this conviction, the persecution, injustice, resentment, and tears you experience are not merely personal. They represent heaven, the angelic world, and the millions of saints who look toward the center of goodness. Therefore, you can appeal to the entire universe of heaven and earth. It is from this point that God's providence has developed.  
From now on, in every action and every word, you must reflect God's heart. You must also resolve the grievances of the angelic world and repay the historical enemies of your ancestors. Thus, we must save this world where evil is rampant. This is the hope of the saints, and you must take responsibility in front of that hope.  
You, who are in such a position, must not allow God to be God, the spiritual realm to be the spiritual realm, and the countless saints to be merely saints. If they wish for their desires to be fulfilled on earth, and if they have no relationship with you, then you are merely an individual. If the spiritual realm were to mobilize and cooperate with such a person, the consequences would be dire. God cannot take responsibility for such a person, nor can He cooperate with them.  
Therefore, if you wish for the cooperation of the spiritual realm, the cooperation of God, and to receive God's protection in accordance with His will, you must always align your heart with God's and the hearts of the spirits of the righteous. Thus, every time you stand before the will, your body and mind must always be in the position of Abraham offering a sacrifice, in the position of Jesus praying in Gethsemane, and in the position of carrying the cross toward Golgotha in the final moments of His decision. You must stand in the position of representing heaven, representing earth, and standing in the position of resolving all grievances of heaven.  
The Right Offering  
God has longed for this reality. The angelic world has also awaited this reality. Our ancestors have longed for the time when this reality would manifest and for the day of atonement that could establish such a reality. Therefore, we must carry out the judgment to remove evil by practicing this tremendous mission with our hands, our mouths, and our bodies. We must walk the path where we can establish goodness and eliminate evil. We must have this unwavering conviction as we move forward.  
Moreover, you who are gathered here must never lose this perspective as you go out to take responsibility and act. There may be times when loneliness seeps into your heart without you realizing it. At such times, you must understand that this loneliness is not your own but the loneliness that God experiences, the loneliness that the angelic world experiences, and the loneliness that our ancestors experience. In those moments, you should be able to enter that heart and shed tears together.  
That place is a profoundly solemn place. When God's heart is reflected in my heart, kneeling there and shedding tears with God, that world filled with love is the most sacred world.  
In this world, where evil is rampant, the place where we rise as holy saints for heaven and worry for the earth is not a place where countless ancestors come to spit. Such a place may appear miserable and insignificant, but it is a holy place where heaven and earth become friends and can discuss everything together. When one becomes such a person, even if there are moments of persecution and suffering, they are temporary. Through that, one can atone for the suffering of the spiritual realm and the suffering of God.  
And by participating in the suffering of the saint and forgetting one's own resentment for the sake of the whole, that becomes a condition for judgment, allowing even the suffering of the saint to be atoned for.  
As our Unification Church has walked the three-year and four-year courses, standing in positions where we could not eat properly, faced persecution, suffered, and struggled, for whom has this been? For whom am I enduring this? I have come out as a sacrifice until now; for whom has that been? First, it is for heaven, then for the angelic world, and then for the millions of saints and our descendants who will be established as hope on this earth. Yes, I have been a sacrifice.  
A sacrifice must have no concept of ownership. It is not about moving forward solely for one's own purpose but about stepping into the place of sacrifice for the sake of the whole, whether it be for a nation or otherwise. Therefore, a sacrifice must not establish personal goals but must establish public goals. It must serve as a stepping stone and foundation to eliminate evil and establish the ideals of goodness. This is the principle we must understand.  
Among you, there may be those who have wept in silence. Holding onto the roots of grass,  
"O God! Please resolve my grievances," or holding onto a stone,  
"You alone know." You may have appealed to know God's hope when He created the world, to know the sorrow of God when Adam and Eve fell, and to know what kind of enemy the angel who caused their fall is before God.  
In such a position, if you have fought on behalf of your nation and taken responsibility for that village, that township, that county, and that province, you must recognize that this is not a place where you alone grieve and appeal. The more you are in such a position, the more you must grieve for the will and humanity, appeal for humanity, and fight on behalf of humanity. You must fight in such a position with the cooperation of heaven.  
Receiving does not lead to restoration.  
God does not come with a false heart to establish a center on earth. He chooses a heart that is of His flesh, of His bones, and of His marrow, focusing on establishing a single emotional center. This position is truly genuine. This is a once-in-history event; without the utmost passion and the deepest heart, one cannot establish a true standard of unity. That is why God has come personally, as a family, as a nation, and globally.  
So, what kind of people are we today? We are those who have been chosen due to such traditional connections, and our hearts, blood, and flesh must be imbued with that ideology and tradition.  
To save one person, we must invest our hearts to replace the heart that God had when He sought individuals, families, nations, and the world.  
What emotional standard have you stood on until now? If you do not meet this principled standard of tradition, the more numerous you are, the more confusion you will bring. The more people gather here, the more they will cause greater distress before God. God desires a true heart unity ideology, which is why He comes to give and seeks to find. Therefore, we who uphold that will must also be true.  
You must not lie in the position you have received from God while going out to evangelize. Jacob could take everything from Laban because his 21 years of sacrifice became the basis for receiving hundreds of times more. The Israelites could take many possessions when they left Egypt because, due to 400 years of hard labor, God could guarantee it, and an internal foundation was established that Satan could acknowledge. Before that, it cannot happen. You must stand in such a position. Therefore, you must appeal to God.  
You must say,  
"I want to give true life. I want to give hundreds of times more than I have received." You must also say, "Satan, you know this, so you cannot accuse me." You must set such conditions to avoid trouble.  
Restoration is not about receiving; the path of restoration is about pioneering. You cannot achieve the history of restoration by receiving from the world of Satan. You must give from heaven. What must you give? You must give true heart, true character, and true words.  
To do this, you must establish the standard of true words, the standard of true character, and the standard of true heart. You must establish true words, true character, and true heart on personal, family, national, and global levels. The one who comes as a responsible figure to broaden this scope and establish the standard of atonement for the entire world is the Messiah. You must not forget that He comes centered on a serious historical background.  
You must feel that even if you are alone in such a position, you are not alone. Even if you go alone, you are not alone. No matter how lonely the situation may be, you are not alone. Even if there is no reason to suffer in every circumstance, you must atone for everything and restore the good position. At that time, if enemies invade, God will strike them.  
That is why you must inherit the heart of God that comes to you, and you must inherit the hearts of the angelic world and the millions of saints on earth. When you stand in such a position, God always takes responsibility.  
When you are trained in such a position and receive God's approval, even if you bear the sins of the world, you can overcome them freely.  
Where did Jesus find the heart to forgive the sins of the world? It was because He stood on a psychological foundation that could transcend everything centered on historical heart. Therefore, all the sins of the world were in a position to be judged by Him. In this way, Jesus could exercise authority over the sins of the world freely. Likewise, you too are individuals, but you stand not as individuals but as the historical reality of resurrection.  
If it is not true, it cannot remain in history.  
So why do I take responsibility and walk this path? It is to give to all humanity. However, since you cannot give everything at once, you give to one individual, and from that individual, it extends to family, tribe, nation, and ultimately to the world. This is God's heart.  
Therefore, when you give today, you must stand in the subjective position, that is, in the position of being the substantial representative of God, so you must be able to see your counterpart accurately. You must discern whether that counterpart is someone who will bring failure before the standard you have established or someone who stands in the position of betraying our ancestors.  
Once you take responsibility, the next step is battle, struggle. You must engage in a fight to see whether you will be broken or whether they will be broken. In that struggle, you must lay the groundwork to naturally subdue at least three or more people who are in an opposing position to you.  
You must understand that God does not use means or methods. You must also not stand in a position to receive throughout your life. Before the will, you must only stand in the position of giving.
Until today, the teacher has prayed for this land even from the position of fighting.  
"Father, this is my country and my land. Although this place is where countless people have rebelled against heaven, where the historical fate of this nation has been blocked, and where the ideology of unification has been led down the path of suffering, what will you do with this land?"  
According to the principle of restoration through indemnity, if they are not subdued here on this land, countless nations will automatically follow evil. That is why we must stand here. We must pray more earnestly for this land than any established Christian praying for their own church.  
The leaders of established churches must fight against the enemy Satan with conviction and present the issue of life and death. This is not a simple matter. It must continue through first, second, and third stages. When you gather in various places in South Korea for God's will on this foundation, God is providing behind you, and countless saints, angels, and your good ancestors are watching your movements as an individual.  
Therefore, the fate of the Unification Church rests on your shoulders. Not only the fate of the Unification Church but also the fate of this nation and the world rests on your shoulders.  
You must establish yourself at this tremendous focal point and walk with God, and walk with humanity as God desires. Such people will be defended by God in front of their correct posture.  
You must pray, "Father, I wish to be a heavenly representative who can find my tribe and my nation by centering on me, as you have made sacrifices to find the central individual of your providence."  
How solemn is this prayer? Isn't it God's wish to establish such people in every region of this land?  
Today, we must carry out this work with such a solemn sense of mission. Let us endure, and let us win, giving truth with blood and sweat before humanity. If it is not true, it cannot remain in history.  
You may not know, but the teacher who sent you has a responsibility. The teacher cannot help but worry that your movements may leave a blemish before the whole and bring about undesirable results.  
We have come to understand that if we leave the masses who do not know God's will alone, God must carry a heavy sigh.  
Despite facing a flat era where we can be established on the same standard, and being a people who share the same fate, how can this nation become enemies? When we think that our ancestors have become enemies, and that the loyal patriots who were faithful for this country have become enemies, you must forgive them with a big heart. And when you go to established churches, you must pray for them with tears.  
Wherever you go with a heart of peace, peace begins, and where you want to give a sincere heart, truth sprouts. By doing this, something will happen in the silence.  
Human nature moves in one direction. If people move according to their nature, God will cooperate, and since good movements are accompanied by heavenly principles, everything will happen automatically.  
You must think about what kind of heart you will go out with on behalf of this nation in the face of the four-year journey ahead.  
What kind of heart did Abraham have when he offered sacrifices? What kind of heart did Jacob have when he offered sacrifices? What kind of heart did Moses have when he went to Pharaoh's palace? And what kind of heart did Jesus have when he went up to the Garden of Gethsemane? You must understand that heart.  
If I have received the overall responsibility from God and have received the command to carry out that responsibility, and I have commanded you to take on such responsibilities for Daegu, but there is no one to carry it out, how lonely would that be?  
Jesus wanted to unify heaven and earth and lay the foundation of victory to command all nations, and although God hoped that day would come quickly, when Jesus could not stand in such a position, God felt deep sorrow and pain. You must understand this.  
What kind of heart have you fought with for the will until now? You must know whether everything you have fought for until now is recognized as being in line with the flow of God's history and the flow of God's heart, or whether it is recognized as being in opposition. You must also think about whether you have the confidence and conviction to be able to do so in the future.  
After this Daegu gathering, you will return. In a few days, you will return. Through the activities you have done in Daegu this time, we must restore the established church. Just as Jesus commanded his disciples to go for Israel, at this time, we must restore the national Cain and internal Cain on the foundation we have built so far. That responsibility lies with us. If we know that flow before them and stand on the path of that flow, restoration will happen automatically.  
Know that you are the ones who represent the heart of God who comes to find you. The teacher is also in the position of going to God, so he must receive God's heart, and since he has shared God's responsibility, he must receive God's heart to fulfill that responsibility.  
We must walk the path where we can say, "I go to fulfill the substance of the Father's wish, the substance of our ancestors' wish; Father, historical ancestors, accompany us!" When you go while feeling such a heart, that place will shine even more.  
The more you feel sorrow, the greater God's grace is in proportion to that sorrow. This inverse phenomenon will appear wherever you go.  
When you shed tears, those tears can represent the tears of the nation, and when you stand in that place, you can represent the national repentance. What the teacher desires is for you to become such people. Such people will never perish. But the question is how patiently you endure.  
"I have gone through the historical course of not being able to establish a day of restoration, which is God's wish! The deeper the valley of darkness, the more I will go deeper into the valley." You must go silently. Then God can say, "Hey, go slowly," and the ancestors can encourage you to go well for us, and the spirit world can guarantee it. How holy such footsteps are!  
Let us walk the path protected by God.  
What the teacher is currently worried about is fulfilling the responsibilities that must be done in this three-year course. There have been many times when I stood in a position of indescribable misery, without friends or companions. However, I tried to go anywhere with God. Because I communicate with God.  
We will someday shed our flesh and go to the spirit world. Therefore, we who were born into this world must be prepared for death. Also, to establish the good self in the eternal world as the second self, we must suffer. Just as a healthy and good baby is born only when it receives good prenatal education in the mother's womb, life in this earthly world is similar to life in the womb. Therefore, we must grow by imitating God's image, God's heart, and God's holy divinity. We must grow and risk our lives to cross over.  
Only by standing in such a position can we become like Abel, who offered sacrifices, like Abraham, who wandered to find a place to offer sacrifices, like Moses, who was preparing to lead the Israelite nation, and like Jesus, who walked a miserable path for 30 years. Thus, you must be able to protect yourselves more than to protect yourselves; God must be able to protect you. You must be able to stand in such a position. To do that, you must not only receive but also give.  
The reason God raised Jacob was to give to his nation and descendants, and the reason God raised Moses and Jesus was not to receive but to give. It is to give something greater. With such a heart, you must live truthfully, abandoning falsehood. Those who cannot do so will naturally perish. When the time comes, people will surely be prepared. God prepares people and carries out His providence.  
When you go out to give on behalf of God's heart, God will be with you behind you. God called Noah and said, "Noah, hurry and find your family." He raised Abraham and said, "Abraham, quickly find your family." He raised Jacob and said, "Hurry and establish a nation." He told Moses to find the nation of Israel. He also told Jesus to find the nation of Israel, the world, and heaven and earth. In this way, God desires to give something greater. However, God opens the way for Israel to be established based on the conditions of indemnity that they can fulfill to establish Israel.  
If the world has entered into a global restoration era today, if it has entered into a cosmic restoration era, then God has already established the conditions for cosmic indemnity. God does not come to impose all burdens on His sons and daughters. Although God has spiritually prepared everything, the responsibility that must be fulfilled in reality lies with humanity. Therefore, humanity must walk with God according to the foundation that God has prepared. When that happens, God will grant the foundation of victory to humanity. This is a great honor.  
When you engage in activities, you will come to understand what time it is. We must carry the family, tribe, and nation on our backs from the position of representing God for the world. We must walk the path that God can guarantee from beginning to end. You must carry out your activities diligently with this mental attitude during the remaining three days. Do you understand? It cannot be done with means and methods.  
We must always work hard in the world. If we lay the foundation for national victory and establish all conditions for national indemnity, that is, if we lay the foundation for victory on this land, then such a foundation will automatically be established in heaven as well. Such a time will come in the future. If the Republic of Korea takes responsibility, God will lead the world to victory based on that national victory standard.  
The teacher goes out with such a heart. Let us endure until that time. Jesus has endured for 2,000 years, and God has endured for 6,000 years. Likewise, we must endure until we establish the standard of global victory. Thus, it is enough to establish only the global standard. Therefore, you must remember that you must mature your heart as you go forward. Do you understand? You must pray like that.  
Restoration history begins from the lowly.  
Every time the teacher prayed for the will, God was with him, the angelic world was with him, and the good ancestors were with him. Likewise, you must not go alone. You must go together. When that happens, you gain strength. You gain the strength to overcome all environments. However, you must not start from the high places. You must start from the lowest places. Only then will there be no crowd.  
Since it is a restoration providence, we must start from the lowly. By doing so, we must later breathe life into it. With the heart of a parent, we must become the body of a servant, shedding blood, sweat, and tears to enable them to follow us.  
You have come out on behalf of God until now. You have dedicated yourself to the nation for the past three years. The teacher is the same, but the Unification Church has faced opposition from the nation until now. However, we must establish dignity before heaven and earth in every aspect, both personally and in terms of our love for the country.  
The conditions to cross over to the world are now connected to us. We are connected to the nation based on a national standard and are connected globally. Therefore, during this four-year course, we must go beyond the national conditions of indemnity. This is the path we are taking. While we are walking this vertical path of indemnity in terms of the church, when viewed individually, the horizontal path of indemnity and restoration is unfolding centered around you.  
Since we are organizing a new tribe and nation centered on the Unification Church, you must go through the horizontal path of indemnity and restoration at the personal, family, tribal, and national levels.  
You must understand that your activities today, standing in such a position, greatly influence the horizontal restoration of indemnity. Do you understand what I mean? If one person joins in and participates in the activities, how will it be when it surpasses the national indemnity standard from the national indemnity? If that happens, not only their ancestors but also those who have a true heart living in the present will somehow cooperate according to the heavenly fortune. Moreover, the spirits in the spirit world will actively cooperate.  
You, who are in the position of being responsible for restoration and indemnity, must know that your good ancestors are in a position like the angels of the angelic world. That is why, just as many angels had to obey Adam before the fall and establish the way of loyalty before him, your good ancestors and loyal patriots are moving to establish the way of loyalty before you. Therefore, the reactions that appear to them will vary according to the degree of our movements.  
When you step forward to take on national responsibility, you must be able to declare.  
"I will firmly attach myself to the fortune of the Unification Church while carrying out the national and ethnic mission centered on an individual and family that God desires and wishes to use." I am a branch of the Unification Church that is growing normally, receiving the fortune of the Unification Church. Therefore, the words of the Unification Church are my words, the personality of the Unification Church is my personality, and the heart of the Unification Church is also my heart.  
If you do that, no matter where you are, you will develop just like the Unification Church. If you establish such a standard and align yourself with the Unification Church, the good spirits and ancestors in the spirit world who have moved according to the national fortune will work for you.  
When you become the branch of victory,  
You may appear to have a flat face and ears that are tucked in, looking unfortunate, but in the spirit world, you are recognized as blessed. Moreover, the ancestors within the ten generations are tightening their hearts. This is because the restoration history is centered on the ten generations. However, if an evil descendant appears, the ancestors within the ten generations will say, "Hey! You are trying to ruin us!"
I will do it.  
Therefore, if descendants with good ancestors are here, the ancestors actively cooperate. You are in such a position. When you, who are in such a position, fight passionately and splendidly, establishing records of victory everywhere, the spiritual world will rejoice forever and ever. When you become such individuals, even evil spirits will be astonished and fall down. That is how it is. Therefore, these ancestors will serve you as if they were serving a king. You must feel this.  
Today, we must lay the foundation for victory with the heart of "Will we defile God's will? Will we defile God's dignity?" You must pray about what kind of tradition you will establish. Now is a blessed time.  
Looking at the restoration history centered on the Israelite people, we can see that unless there were ancestors who faced the will with faith and good relationships, and loyal subjects who were devoted to God, Jesus could not have appeared in that era. In this way, the ancestors laid the foundation first.  
Similarly, in today's restoration history, with the emergence of the Unification Church in Korea centered on the will, a time has come where we can indemnify the vertical history and unfold it horizontally. Therefore, if you achieve heart unity, character unity, and word unity before the will, you will be able to unfold the vertical history horizontally. Do you understand this relationship?  
In the time of Jesus, because he came to the earth, the good ancestors from before were able to enter the life-form spiritual realm conditionally. Likewise, your ancestors have entered a special privilege to be able to return through you, who are on the earth. Do you understand what I mean? When you understand this will and become branches of victory, you are in a position to form a life entity, which is why your ancestors are cooperating with you. In this way, you must become the foundation upon which thousands of generations of good ancestors can return.  
In the time of Jesus, the spiritual realm cooperated conditionally for the resurrection of life forms, but now is a time when the spiritual realm cooperates unconditionally for the resurrection of life forms. Because this time has come, there is no greater blessing than this. Do you understand what I mean? In other words, the spiritual realm is cooperating.  
Therefore, from now on, the search for tribes will speed up. Because historical connections are established, the conditions for cooperation are also established, which is why it will speed up. The Unification Church must fight to resolve the conflicts among divided religions and sects. Right now, all religions are fighting against each other, and Christianity is in conflict. Therefore, you must fight throughout your lives to unite the divided sects and fight for this nation. We must welcome a united nation and state.  
The Messiah is the ancestor of the word, the ancestor of character, the ancestor of heart.  
The teacher dislikes people who wander alone. When I look at you, you seem to wander around doing whatever you want and saying all sorts of things, but that should not be the case.  
How holy would it be if we could raise the resurrection on the earth? If there are loyal subjects, virtuous women, or filial sons among your ancestors, they will come when you call them in prayer. Because now the ancestors must cooperate with you. That is how it is.  
If a group going up in one direction is made to go up in another direction, the one who was last will be first. When going up like this, the one who was last to stand will also be the first to come down.  
Until now, Satan has gone ahead, but if we change direction as just mentioned, Satan will be last, and we will be at the forefront.  
We must establish God's heart so that Satan's advance can be indemnified and we can make a new start. The representative who does this is the Messiah. Therefore, the Messiah is the ancestor of the word, the ancestor of character, and the ancestor of heart.  
You should not pray for yourselves in the future. You should not go to God and say, "Oh, Father, I have come. Please bless me. I am pitiful and hungry, so please do something for me." Do not pray such trivial prayers. You should pray, "I have come here to relieve the Father's sorrow; please teach me how to do so." If you pray like this, will He not listen to you? If you only present the conditions under which you can do good, you will pass through safely. Do you understand?  
Ancestors are judged by their descendants.  
Where did the commercial bank basketball team go this time? They went to Peru, right? They fought against the Argentine team and won by 87 to 50-something, right? How happy the Korean residents there must have been! They avenged the sorrow of being treated as outsiders until now. They can now speak loudly. The same goes for the will. Your ancestors are the same. When you win in all aspects of the restoration providence, they will dance and say, "Our descendants have fought and won!"  
You must realize that you are in a position to judge your ancestors. Do you understand what I mean? Your ancestors are to be judged by you. When God judges, He judges both heaven and earth. Therefore, you should not complain carelessly with your grievances. No matter how much you suffer, you cannot complain if you are in a position of responsibility.  
The sins of ancestors must be indemnified by establishing good descendants. Good descendants must be established to cooperate with them.  
Then, there will be faults among the ancestors of each sect, tribe, and clan. How will we indemnify those faults? What will we use for indemnification? We must use offerings, offerings to indemnify. We must place offerings on Abel's altar that can be presented before God.  
Our Unification Church is Abel's altar. We are currently struggling to set up the Abel's altar. Although it is Abel's altar, we must struggle to be offered as sacrifices on Cain's altar. This struggle is the way to indemnify all the sins of our ancestors. Therefore, the altar with Abel's ideology goes through a process of suffering to find an environment that can be presented before heaven. It is precisely because this period is necessary that we speak of seven years or three years. Do you understand?  
Therefore, if you do not want to walk this path, you are betraying history and becoming a traitor to history. In that case, your ancestors will judge you, saying, "You have blocked our path, and you have completely destroyed the achievements we built through our hard work."  
When Jesus entered Jerusalem, he saw a fig tree on the way up the stairs and sent his disciples to seek fruit. When there was no fruit, he cursed the tree, right? Even though it was the same as other trees, he cursed it because it bore no fruit. This fruitless tree symbolizes the saints of the end times.  
God will judge the ancestors of the past at the end. However, God desires that the descendants establish conditions for indemnification. That is why He is withholding judgment. So when will He judge? He will judge after the descendants, who focus on patience, stand on the foundation of victory and establish conditions to move those ancestors to a good position.  
Therefore, you must first do personal indemnification. After personal indemnification, you can participate in family, tribal, or national indemnification. Do you understand? By indemnifying everything from a personal standard, you can contribute to God, who wishes to indemnify on a family level, and to God, who wishes to indemnify on a tribal level. Personal indemnification cannot be neglected. Do you understand? That is why I tell you to suffer. In the future, when you enter the Unification Church, you will all be made to suffer. Is that love, or is it destruction?  
Suffering and indemnification.  
When I look into your eyes, it seems that you have not yet fully experienced suffering. Those who are like that must suffer more. I will drive you onto the path of suffering. It cannot be done with the help of others; you must indemnify through your own suffering.  
Thus, the Israelite people also indemnified their historical sorrows through suffering. Because the entire historical conditions accumulated over 6,000 years have not yet been resolved, the Unification Church and the teacher have emerged today. The teacher does this work for God's sake.  
The descendants must indemnify the sins of their ancestors who have bloodline connections. Otherwise, who will repay them? Who will repay the sins committed by ancestors? Therefore, the descendants must indemnify. To indemnify, they must offer sacrifices centered on Abel's altar and prepare a Cain's altar to offer sacrifices like Cain. This preparation must be made. That is why there is a seven-year course. Do you understand? You must build the Abel's altar while walking the seven-year course and build a national altar. Therefore, you must go forward with absolute obedience.  
Not only in such gatherings, but when the teacher and important members gather together, the ancestors cry out that they are not being included and urgently appeal to be included. They appeal, asking why their grandchildren and children, who attend the Unification Church, are not being included. Not including them becomes an infinite sorrow for them. You may not have known this until now. By continuing to hold such gatherings, the period of indemnifying the sins committed by your ancestors is reduced by hundreds or thousands of years.  
Among your ancestors, there are all kinds of people. When a descendant who does not have good ancestors dedicates themselves and produces results, God will give that person special attention. You must recognize that this is a wonderful period. Do you understand? Raise your hands if you understand.  
In the future, there will come a time when you will want to participate in such gatherings but will not be able to. That time will come. The teacher tells you to suffer because he knows this. No matter how tedious that suffering may be, you must not seek sympathy. If you seek sympathy, it will not be your own.  
The teacher has already done everything he can for you. Therefore, you must not seek sympathy at all. Rather, you should eat only two meals a day instead of three and give one meal to others. You must do this. You must accomplish what could take ten years of suffering in just ten months. We must indemnify all the historical sins of our ancestors during this period. No matter how much you suffer, you must not fall away from the path of the will. You must survive and not die.  
The suffering you have endured until now will lay the foundation for the greatest achievements that can be resurrected based on the principles of indemnification. You must understand this. When that happens, the ancestors in the spiritual realm will be able to connect with many people on the earth, establish relationships with the earthly environment, and create relative standards upon that foundation to return.  
That is why you must now engage in national indemnification. How pleased your ancestors will be when you fulfill your mission! If you cannot go through this path of indemnification, you will not be able to lift your heads before God in the spiritual realm.  
If you live thinking of your body only as an individual body, what will happen? You must understand that your ancestors will be wringing their hands in anguish. Now we must indemnify the individual and tribal aspects and move into the national fortune. Now is the time when the teacher is guiding you into a special privilege. That is why these days, I pray like this:  
"Since there is this principle of indemnification, Father, please allow the ancestors to gain merit through all the tears and sweat until now."  
Indemnification must be done voluntarily.  
The teacher sees that a time will come when he can show you much. It will happen. Now you must understand whether participating in such gatherings is a blessing or not.  
Therefore, you must quickly indemnify everything centered on the individual and the tribe. Even if it takes a hundred deaths and resurrections to condense 6,000 years, it must be done. If it cannot be done in one day, it must be done over ten years or a hundred years. That is why you must not blame anyone. Those who suffer among the Unification Church must not seek sympathy. Even if they find themselves in an environment where they are not suffering, they will still suffer immensely. This is because they were born into the wrong lineage of ancestors.  
Even if you try to make someone who does not suffer suffer every day, those who are born that way will end up in a better position. Why is that? It is because the spiritual realm has prepared a foundation for cooperation. If you go to the spiritual realm as you are now, it will be a big problem.  
No matter what difficulties arise on the earth, you must resolve those difficulties. So, should you move or not?  
When you think about going through the history of indemnification, this path is not one that someone can tell you to go or not go. If you do not go, it is the one who does not go who will perish, not the teacher or the Unification Church. If you do not go, you will now enter a global era, and people from around the world will be brought to you. The global fortune is now converging on Korea.  
Who are you? Are you the children of God? Are you really the children of God? Look at your mouths and noses. Look closely. Is this what a child of God looks like? What kind of child! You are no different from the people of the world. Even those who believe well in the Unification Church are not much better than the people of the world. However, if you properly qualify yourselves, you will be better than the Pacific Ocean.  
You must become children who cannot be exchanged for heaven and earth. However, that does not happen automatically. There must be harmony of heaven and earth, or a great upheaval of heaven and earth, or some event must occur. That is why the teacher is trying to raise the great work of heaven and earth centered on your tribes.  
If a grandfather cannot do what a grandson can do, where is the greater upheaval of heaven and earth? If a few generations of ancestors are instead called grandfather by a grandson from a few generations below, where is the greater upheaval of heaven and earth? Such events will occur now.  
Therefore, you must never think that you are going along in a flat manner from a personal standpoint. You must gladly accept the suffering you endure. If you gladly accept the suffering, your ancestors will be liberated. Therefore, you must learn to gladly accept any suffering. Those who walk this path and win after suffering can liberate countless ancestors.  
Let us indemnify quickly.  
You can live the life of a farmer as well as anyone else. You will also achieve the merit of the nation. We must become the Unification Church that engages in national indemnification through such processes. We must take responsibility for national indemnification and the national sorrow with all our sincerity. We must be the first to suffer, to be insulted, and to endure hardship.  
In the next four years, all those in administrative positions must decide whether to believe in the Unification Church or not. From now on, we must lead democracy centered on conscientious people. Now is the time to establish the correct path of faith and indemnification.
You must recognize that it is time to go through the process of restoration.  
In the future, our Unification Church members must go to countless nations on the global path of indemnity and start from servitude, leading them to believe in God. Those who serve God must do this. They must instill the awareness that they should emulate this solemn tradition, as the ancestors of humanity have suffered first.  
When everyone looks up to us, then we will be able to eat a hundred cows a day and be told to eat more, and even if we change clothes a thousand times a day, we will be told to change again. At that time, we will achieve the restoration of all things.  
Even though you may look shriveled and shabby now, if you are well-prepared and have dimensionality both inside and out, you will appear beautiful. The beauty of that time is the highest beauty that cannot be exchanged for the universe. Even from the Teacher's perspective, it is so, and it will be even more so from God's perspective. If you possess such qualities, everything in heaven and earth will be within you. When you look into someone's eyes, you can see the sorrow of heaven and earth, and wherever you look at their hands or feet, you will find something that represents heaven and earth. The Teacher's intention is to create such masterpieces.  
When the Teacher was young like you, he used to buy cheap clothes that others had thrown away from junk shops. He wore clothes that smelled so bad that young ladies could not follow him. He wore clothes that made people want to run away when they got close. A man of the Unification Church should be carefree. Even if there is a hole in his socks, he should be dignified.  
Just as a great mountain is home to various trees and colorful birds and animals, you too must have something that can house everything within you. Only then can you maintain your overall posture, and that will manifest as a kind of beauty. It is not beautiful just because you wear nice clothes or because you are well-prepared. You must become a person who can become a topic of conversation and an object of envy in heaven and earth. How magnificent would such a being be? Isn’t that so? I intend to start a new trend among our Unification Church members.  
What is considered beautiful forever is the original beauty. We must create a world that flows like water, harmonizing with heaven and earth and the true rhythm of harmony. What this man here desires is for us to quickly achieve indemnity.  
You have gathered here with great effort to overcome the satanic world. You are working for the first time in history as the heavenly soldiers to conquer the satanic world.  
Go through the four-year course with the heart of a new start.  
When God dances, I must also dance so that heaven and earth can burst into laughter and create joy. Speaking of dancing, these days, when asked to dance, people twist and turn, right? This is all the work of Satan. What does it mean to twist like a taffy? It is a snake, right? Therefore, this era is the last stage of entering the satanic world. Now, we must tell those who dance like that to take a break.  
You must unravel the path of indemnity. From personal indemnity to national indemnity, there is a fateful path that you must take, so you must go quickly.  
In the next four years, I will make you suffer a bit more. The path of direct progress is the way to receive the greatest blessings. The Teacher has realized this fact. This means I am aware of it.  
If I had not become the Teacher of the Unification Church, I would not have done such things. However, knowing the purpose, I want everyone to restore themselves. I am setting standards and working hard. However, when you eat, eat to your fill. Do you know how to suffer when you are hungry? Do you know how to endure pain? You will suffer to the extent that the Grandfather of Suffering would praise you. The Grandfather of Suffering would send you off with a tag saying, "You have now suffered all this suffering." Originally, you should come to the Unification Church after having suffered like this. Therefore, you must quickly go through indemnity. The Teacher makes you suffer because he loves you. He cannot give you blessings without making you suffer.  
To walk this path, you must have true faith and become a sacrifice. How much you can indemnify depends on your determination, activities, and actions. Therefore, each of you must recognize that you must become a valuable existence. When you do that, you can become the sons and daughters of God. So during this period, there should be a struggle at the door to see who will go out first.  
If you are going to fight, you should fight with great people. I must be the first to accumulate the best results. You must have this mindset, and you must vigorously cross the four-year course for the return to your hometown. You must take this opportunity to have the strength to make a new start.  
I will also go. This is the wish of the Teacher for you. If you do not rise again this time, the Teacher will be separated from you.  
During this period when the Teacher is moving together with you, you must rise again and evoke the feelings and determination you had when you first understood the purpose and received grace. Without doing so, you cannot go through the four-year course to the end. You must know this and somehow participate in this path of suffering and run toward the path you must take.

Based on your victorious conditions, you can liberate the spirit world, so do not think of yourselves as individual beings but rather as those who should be loyal. You must carry out the national indemnity.

If we only pave the foundation for the nation, God will work greatly. We must be grateful for these historical benefits. How grateful it is to be persecuted for the purpose? Let us keep the items used for the purpose well and be loyal in all aspects centered on the purpose and express our gratitude with sincerity.

If one works hard to repay others' debts rather than their own, they can quickly achieve indemnity. We need people who are willing to risk death to repay the debts owed to heaven. We need an attitude that cares for the debts that all humanity must repay.

The heart is the essence, and the body is the form; thus, the form exists to realize the essence. This is like Cain and Abel; the established church is in the position of Cain, and the Unification Church is in the position of Abel. If Abel wins, God wins. This is the victory of the three dimensions.

Work Responsibly for the Purpose

Heaven and earth have come to find humanity, and God has come to find humanity, but humanity did not know that.  
God's sorrow lies in the fact that there are no true children who understand and serve His heart. What God desires is true children whose hearts resonate with His. Since the time of offerings, we have desired a heart-centered world centered on the Father. God has longed for loyal subjects and virtuous women, and He wanted Noah, Abraham, and Moses to be loyal subjects. Because God's will through Jesus failed, He has a grievance. Therefore, we, who are within the historical benefits, must unite our hearts with the returning Lord and fulfill the purpose.  
Let us become models of loyalty and filial piety before heaven for the sake of our nation and humanity. To resolve the historical grievances with our own substance, our lives must align with the purpose and perspective centered on heaven.
