**  
<April 28, 1964 (Tuesday), 6 AM, Daegu Front Mountain Sanctuary.>  
* These words were given after the conclusion of the Third Principle Workshop held in Daegu, gathering all members at the Daegu Front Mountain Sanctuary, and have been compiled from the publication in <Gyeonggi Frontline> No. 7. The title was added by the editor.  
**  
Our Unification Church members must overcome the established church to fulfill the purpose.  
The blood of Abel cries out from the ground, and we must resolve that grievance.  
We must endure suffering from three nations and from the three sovereigns and win over the three great tests of Satan to be resurrected. This revival meeting is the battle against the established church, which represents Judaism and Israel, on the foundation of victory.  
God is with us, so we must have the courage to fight.  
We must have the conviction that even if heaven and earth change, I remain unchanging. We must be filled with the conviction that I will indemnify Abel's grievance, which is deeply rooted in history, heaven, and earth, and create the history of heaven tomorrow. We must be filled with the conviction that we will resolve God's grievance and fulfill the purpose on behalf of Jesus. Heaven and earth are both the Father's and ours.  
The tide has changed, and now we cannot be persecuted.  
The misery of the people starving and struggling in the mountains is akin to God's past position. When we see the suffering people, we must hold their hands and weep. Those who should become God's children are oppressed before their enemies, so we must weep upon seeing their misery. Even if you are starving, do not lose heart; you must become loyal subjects who weep for them. You must be children who can weep on behalf of God's and the Father’s heart.
to restore the original purpose of creation. 

From the day humans fell, the history of suffering, sadness, and misery began on this earth. This is not the original purpose that God planned at the time of creation. God did not want such a world, and humans did not wish to be born and live in such a world. For this reason, God has sought to resolve this miserable history, this sad and painful history, and restore the original hope He had.

The suffering of Jesus, who came to this earth, is a reflection of God's heart. Jesus, who was sent as the Prince of Heaven and the Savior of all humanity, lived a life filled with sorrow and pain. He faced persecution and opposition from those He came to save. His life was a testament to the deep love and longing of God for humanity, yet it was also marked by the rejection and betrayal of those He sought to redeem.

In this context, we must understand the significance of Jesus' suffering. It was not merely a historical event but a profound expression of God's desire to reconcile with humanity. Through His pain, Jesus demonstrated the depth of God's love and the lengths to which He would go to restore the relationship between Himself and His creation.

As we reflect on the life of Jesus, we are reminded of our own responsibilities. We are called to carry on the mission that Jesus began, to bring hope to the hopeless, to comfort the afflicted, and to work towards the unity that God desires for all of creation. 

In conclusion, let us remember the suffering of Jesus and the love of God that it represents. May we strive to embody that love in our own lives, working towards a world that reflects God's original purpose for humanity.
the world of peace, the world of happiness, the world of freedom, and the world of goodness. You are setting a purpose to reclaim these worlds and are working to restore this fallen world. This is the path of restoration and the path of salvation providence.

In order to carry out salvation, God, who governs, does not take a negligent stance that merely observes all the suffering on this earth. Therefore, He does not merely stand by as humans endure all the suffering in this fallen world; rather, He enters directly into the realm of that suffering, taking responsibility and responding to it. 

Moreover, without God's direct participation in this sad and miserable historical process, humanity cannot be saved. Thus, God has been fighting alongside humanity throughout its sorrowful history until now. 

How should we save this land? God's wish is to save the entire world at once based on an overall standard. However, since the entire fallen world cannot stand before God's will, He is laying the groundwork and raising chosen individuals to restore one family, tribe, nation, and world, in that order. By doing so, He is creating an environment and historical background in which He can govern from an overall standard, aiming to achieve the wish and purpose of the completion of restoration through salvation.

So, what kind of era were the times of Noah, Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob in the historical process? They were eras centered on individuals and families. Based on this providential era of individuals and families, the Israelite people were to establish a national integrity according to God's laws, which were set by the traditions and emotional foundations that God had formed with them. This was the mission of the chosen Israelite people. However, they failed to establish such integrity, could not uphold the traditions inherited from God, and did not fulfill their historical mission. As a result, they fell and could not achieve God's promised national restoration during the 400 years of oppression in Egypt.

Thus, God raised Moses to fulfill His purpose, and later, He sought to accomplish it through Joshua and Caleb. However, the Israelite people who entered the land of Canaan could not become a nation capable of completing national restoration in their time and, due to their lack of suitable conditions, God raised many prophets throughout the ages to lead the nation. After going through the period of the judges, the reigns of King Saul, King David, and King Solomon, and the division of the northern and southern kingdoms, God worked through the 210 years of Babylonian captivity and the preparation period for the coming of the Messiah to establish the standard for national restoration. There was a divine effort made by God to prepare a foundation for sending Jesus.

On this national foundation, Judaism, which had established a sovereign nation and formed the internal basis of national spirit and thought, was to unite with the Israelite people and complete the standard for national restoration by integrating the twelve tribes of Israel. This was the mission of the Israelite people until the coming of Jesus. However, the Israelite people and Judaism failed to establish the foundation for national restoration. Consequently, the foundation for receiving Jesus was destroyed, and we must understand that Jesus could not complete His mission of global restoration.

If the Israelite people had united with Judaism to establish a foundation for national victory and simultaneously determined a national foundation that could complete God's providence of restoration and salvation, and had presented it before the coming Messiah, then Jesus could have stood in a position to govern and lead the entire nation. Based on that, He would have embarked on the global path of restoration. That was God's ideal when He sent the Messiah.

However, the Israelite people did not recognize the Messiah, nor did they understand the purpose of the Messiah and the will of God who sent Him. If God's will and the national wish of Israel had aligned and connected with the Messiah, then God's historical will would have been fulfilled, and the national wish would have been realized. Thus, the Israelite people were to appear as a blessed priestly people with the ideals that God had blessed in the new era. However, because they did not understand God's hope in sending the Messiah and could not unite with Him, Jesus had to walk the path of the cross.

As a result, what has happened to history until now? Because the national foundation for the restoration of Israel was not established, a new national standard emerged, and after going through the foundation of the nation, it has been connected to the entire world through Christianity today. This is what we must understand as the 2,000-year history of Christianity.

What is the purpose of God's providence in this way? It is to establish an overall standard to restore this universe to the world of God's ideal creation purpose. That has been the providence that God has led for 6,000 years.

The Messiah has already come and gone 2,000 years ago. When He came to this earth, He had His own hopes and circumstances. The one who came to this earth had the responsibility to establish a connection of divine love that could not be severed by the forces of evil between God and humanity.

Nevertheless, because the Israelite people betrayed Him, Jesus was driven and chased, carrying the cross to Golgotha, and He could not pass on His hopes, His circumstances, or His heart to anyone on this earth. The hope He sought to realize on earth, the heart He sought to establish on earth, was carried away along with the cross, and this is something that all Christians around the world must understand.

Today, believers on this earth, we who are facing the end times, must reflect once again on the time of Jesus 2,000 years ago. What if the Israelite people and Judaism had fulfilled their responsibilities at that time? They could have started the global path of restoration with the ideals of a worldwide religion based on the Israelite people and Judaism. That was God's wish when He sent the Messiah. However, because they failed to fulfill their responsibilities, Jesus' death on the cross resulted in only spiritual restoration, that is, spiritual salvation. Therefore, connecting that national foundation and bringing it out to a global scale is the history of restoration providence until now.

So, did God intend to send Jesus to this earth and place Him in a sad position? Absolutely not.

The position Jesus should have been in
God prepared for a new day for 4,000 years, even putting many prophets in situations of death, to send a savior who could dominate the world as a new leader in a new era, nation, and world. He protected the chosen Israelite people, centered on Jacob, through numerous trials, and led them to fulfill the promise of a new day until the time of Jesus. Did God send Jesus to place Him in a sad position? We must understand that this is absolutely not the case.

Then, what was Jesus' mission? What position should He have lived in, and what kind of life should He have led? Jesus did not come to live as a carpenter's assistant in a carpenter's household. He was not to be born in a stable. Where had the Israelite people, who had been prepared for 4,000 years, gone that they treated the Messiah who came so contemptibly? Why did they fail to recognize Him and treat Him so poorly? Why did they have to welcome the Messiah, who came as the King of Kings, in such a miserable position? This was not God's purpose in sending Jesus after 4,000 years of preparation.

The Israelite people should have welcomed the Messiah sent by God into the royal palace of their nation, with the priests and scribes at the center, and numerous clergy welcoming Him as their king in a position of glory above themselves. That was the place where the Messiah, who was the hope of the Israelite people, should have stayed. That was God's wish when He sent the Messiah to this earth.

However, Jesus, who came as the Messiah, was born in a stable. God, who announced the birth of the Messiah to Mary, did not want the Messiah to be born in such a miserable place. This happened because of human failure.

Yet today, Christians say that Jesus was born in a stable because He had to pave the way from a miserable position to a glorious one to become the Savior of all people. This is absolutely not true.

Jesus should have governed the scribes and consulted with the priests. He should have commanded all people on behalf of the king of that nation. This was the purpose of God in sending the Messiah, and it was the purpose of Jesus, who came to this earth with the mission of being the Messiah. Jesus should have been discussing with the most authoritative people from birth, commanding them, and becoming the main character of judgment capable of seizing a global foundation and overcoming the evil world.

How did Jesus live when He came to this earth? He was insulted and chased away. If He was driven out of one village, He had to flee to another, and if He was driven out of that village, He had to escape to yet another. Such a life was not the life that the Messiah, who had come after 4,000 years of preparation, should have lived. Did God send Jesus to live in such a way?

From the moment He was born, Jesus knew what kind of life He should lead as the Messiah and what the purpose was for which God had sent Him as the Messiah. Jesus' heart was more earnest than that of Moses, who felt the mission to lead the Israelite people out of Egypt and conquer all seven nations of Canaan.

Jesus had the responsibility to strike down all the satanic nations of the world and restore them to God, to repay God's enemies, and to make all people into God's sons and daughters. That was the original responsibility of Jesus, who came to this earth as the Messiah.

However, what was the stage of life for Jesus when He came to this earth? It was miserable. We must recognize that Jesus was in a position worse than any high priest or clergyman of the Jewish people or anyone of that time. He had no place to rest, saying, "Foxes have holes, and birds of the air have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay His head." (Matthew 8:20) He also said, "Who are My mother and My brothers? Whoever does the will of My Father in heaven is My brother and sister and mother." This is a profound statement.

Jesus, born into the household of Joseph, was in such a pitiful state. Although Joseph and Mary received special love from God at the time of Jesus' conception, as time passed and the era changed, their hearts changed drastically from the feelings they had when God sent an angel to announce Jesus' conception.

When Joseph quietly observed Jesus, what kind of child was He? He had heard the voice of God that He was conceived by the Holy Spirit, but He was still a stepson. Joseph's heart had changed in that way. Joseph should have had a heart of loyalty that served Jesus throughout His 30 years of life, praying for Him with a heart devoted to God's will, but instead, he treated Jesus poorly with a human heart.

During the Jewish festivals, Joseph and Mary wanted to give good clothes and good food to Jesus' siblings, but they never thought of giving anything particularly generous to Jesus, the son chosen by God. Jesus walked the path of such a sorrowful and bitter life.

What do we say about Jesus, who came as the Messiah? What do we say about the carpenter's tools, the saw, and the chisel? How could the Messiah be a carpenter's assistant? What kind of preparation period is it to live as a carpenter when He should have been preparing to establish a foundation to take responsibility for the fate of all people along with God?

The reason the Jewish people walked the path of suffering
In a world of darkness, where both the priests and the Israelite people did not understand God's will and did not recognize the Messiah who came, they went in their own twisted direction. How heartbreaking and painful it must have been for Jesus to have to restore them! God sent the Messiah on the foundation of the Israelite people, prepared for 4,000 years, so Jesus had to fight against Satan, achieve God's will, and resolve God's grievances, yet He had no foundation to stand on.

For this reason, Jesus felt unworthy before God. Would a messenger sent by a nation, having failed all responsibilities and duties, have the face to return before the king? If a messenger of a nation feels this way, how much more so would Jesus, who came as the Messiah?

Because the Israelite people and Judaism, who had worked hard for 4,000 years, could not unite to support Jesus, His life became miserable. It was not miserable because He was starving or because He was naked. It was miserable because Jesus, who came for God, felt unworthy before God.

God wanted to connect the historical altar of tears and blood that He had prepared for 4,000 years and pass it on to Jesus, hoping that Jesus would restore it and establish a sovereign nation centered on the people He had set up, ruling over all people with the authority of the King of Kings.

However, Jesus could not even ascend to the throne or stand in the position of a sovereign. Internally, He had the content to command the world, yet He was in a position where He could not do so, suffering more than being chased by traitors and villains. We must understand the sorrow of Jesus today.

Who would have thought that Jesus, who came to this earth as the heavenly prince, would end up in such a miserable and pitiful state? 

The Israelite people, who betrayed the Messiah they had awaited for 4,000 years, have all received punishment. Why did they become a wandering nation that could not establish sovereignty for 2,000 years after Jesus' death? Why did six million Jews perish? They received the punishment they deserved. Because they killed Jesus, this is what ultimately happened. It is the price of their sin in betraying God's will.

They made Jesus a wanderer, so they became a wandering nation. They made Jesus an orphan, so they experienced life like orphans. They made Jesus a fugitive, so they should experience being chased and driven away. They should experience being persecuted and hunted down worldwide.

The failure of the chosen central nation is limited to the flat realm of one nation, but from God's perspective, it is not at all flat or limited. Because the Israelite people killed the Messiah, who represented the world, they must walk the path of global indemnity.

The disbelief of the Israelite people has become God's grievance, and that grievance must be indemnified on this earth so that a new Israelite nation can be established and restored on this earth. This is what we must understand as the end times in God's will.

Although Jesus did not get to be the head of a household when He came to this earth, since the creation of the heavens and the earth...
The one who came to this land possessed a character greater than anyone who has ever set foot here,  
Though he did not experience the responsibilities of a tribal leader, he came as a more excellent leader than any tribal chief in this land. He may not have sat on the throne of a king or emperor, but he bore a greater responsibility than any king or emperor. He had to fulfill that responsibility on this earth to establish the nation that God desired to create at the time of creation, a nation of love, a nation of hope, a nation of freedom and liberation. To achieve such a nation globally all at once, God sent Jesus. But to kill such a Jesus and make people believe in the cross to manage the world?  
Jesus walked the path of life for over 30 years on this earth, but he felt the sorrow that God experienced over 4,000 years of history and drank the bitter cup of defeat on this earth. That is why, at the end, Jesus said he was naked and hungry.  
When Jesus came to this earth, how much did the people of Israel conspire against and betray him? However, Jesus was more saddened by the fact that if he died like that, a tremendous path of suffering would remain for the future believers of the New Testament than by his own suffering. That is why he prayed three times in the Garden of Gethsemane.  
“Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me.” (Matthew 26:39)  
The path that the Lord walked is the path that all humans on this earth must follow. The children must follow the path that the Father walks. As the Father goes to establish a nation, the children must also follow to that nation. While obeying and going to that nation, they must not die even if they stumble along the way. Thus, God established one Messiah toward the final battlefield of world history.  
God's desire in establishing the Messiah is the construction of a good Israel. Therefore, even though the first Israel was destroyed, God established Christianity as the second Israel to form a global Israelite nation, which is democracy. Here, Christianity stands in the same position as Judaism.  
The Desire of Jesus and the Emergence of the Unification Church  
The Lord who came to the land of Judea 2,000 years ago, the history that aimed to establish national sovereignty by welcoming a national Messiah was interrupted, but God's providence cannot be interrupted. From a heavenly standard, even if only externally, a global foundation must be laid and inherited by the democratic camp as the second Israel nation and by Christianity as the second Judaism. For that to happen, Christianity must be unified. If it is not unified, it will perish. If Christianity fails to take on the responsibility of guiding the Israelite nation, it will perish.  
To fulfill such a mission and responsibility, the Unification Church has emerged.  
2,000 years ago, Jesus who came to this earth was supposed to complete the global restoration and become the King of Kings. However, he returned with a grievance, so we must meet on the global stage where the second Israel is to be established and connect the national foundation. We must also establish the second Judaism globally and meet at the national starting point. That is precisely today's Christianity and democracy.  
This responsibility should have been fulfilled during Jesus' time, but it was not. Not even a word could be said about that responsibility. Within Jesus' heart, he must have wondered, “Where are the true filial sons who want to live together in such a nation and want to lead in that nation?” The day when God's will and humanity's hope are fulfilled, he longed for true children who would lead all creation before God and give glory to Him. Although Jesus came with such ideals, he never fulfilled that will. He never even had a chance to say it.  
Jesus said that his own family members were enemies. The neighborhood where I live is an enemy, and the nation where I live is an enemy. Within myself, this body is an enemy. My mother and father are enemies, and my tribe, nation, and this world are enemies.  
When Jesus came to this earth as an orphan, when did he ever express his wishes? It is in the Bible: “I came to cast fire on the earth, and how I wish it were already kindled!” (Luke 12:49). He cast the fire, but it did not ignite. The fire did not catch. How much anguish must have filled his heart? Looking over Jerusalem, he lamented, “O Jerusalem, Jerusalem, the one who kills the prophets and stones those who are sent to her! How often I wanted to gather your children together, as a hen gathers her chicks under her wings, but you were not willing!” (Matthew 23:37). We must understand the sorrowful heart of Jesus.  
In his frustration, he even cursed the Israelite nation. The state of Israel was twisted at that time. Consider Jesus' feelings when he said, “Woe to you, scribes and Pharisees, hypocrites!” (Matthew 23:29).  
For over 30 years, the heart he held within, that inner conviction, was never expressed by Jesus. He had a resolute determination in his heart, but he could not speak it to anyone. What kind of apostles were those dull disciples? Were they apostles who would run away when things got tough?  
They did not represent just one nation. Those called before history did not only represent the nation of Israel and Judaism. They were representatives of the world and all humanity. They were a special task force that emerged to represent all people by God's special command. Yet, they ran away in fear of the sword? They fled for fear of losing their heads? And still, they are called apostles? Jesus was able to call them apostles because he returned after his resurrection and gathered them again. Just three days prior, they had sworn resolutely that they would not abandon the Lord, even if they all had to die. Yet, they turned back and fled. What must have been Jesus' heart when he returned to find them after three days? Would he have rejoiced, saying, “Look, I have come back to life”? No. It was truly a pitiful sight.  
The Unspoken Circumstances of Jesus  
Who entered paradise first? The thief entered first. You must understand this.  
We, the saints who are at the end, must understand the injustices that Jesus faced when he came to this earth. We must understand the circumstances of Jesus' unfairness. He felt wronged because he could not fulfill God's will, and he felt wronged and frustrated because he had many wishes and things he wanted to say on this earth but could not. He could not even say he was in pain after being beaten.  
How could the Son of God become such a pitiful being, driven from the world of Satan? However, Jesus could not show his pitiful state of shedding tears. He had to go on as a loyal servant of God, as a true filial son of God. No matter how much he was beaten and chased, he could not harbor a resentful heart.  
He had to go on as the Son of God with dignity.  
Consider the circumstances of Jesus, who could not fulfill his responsibilities before God, who came to this earth with responsibilities and wishes but could not express them, who had to die with 4,000 years of history while failing to save all humanity. How frustrated he must have been! Even when Jesus shed tears, he did so from a universal perspective, and even while carrying the cross from a universal perspective of misery, he walked on without despair.  
Jesus knew all the historical facts of heaven and earth very well. He knew that if he cursed them, the providence of salvation for humanity would collapse. If Jesus had said, “God, avenge me on my enemies!” the entire nation of Israel would have gone to hell. He knew that by violating Jesus' wishes and God's wishes, if judgment were to come, everyone would have to be swept away.  
However, Jesus knew that the Israelite nation was a nation that God had labored for 4,000 years to establish. He understood how much God had worked to prepare the Israelite nation to anticipate and establish him. That is why he could not curse them. Thus, if they fell, they would be restored and re-established after countless efforts, and the Israelite nation should receive eternal blessings from God on this earth.  
However, Jesus thought, “God has hope for these people and sent me to the land of Israel, and I have lived for them and fought for them for over 30 years. The purpose of fighting for them was to save them, not to punish them. If I curse them here, not only will they go to hell, but their descendants will also go to hell, and the restoration history that has been established until now will all collapse.”  
That is why he prayed three times: “Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not my will, but yours be done.” This was a heartfelt plea. Who understood such a heart of Jesus? Do those who believe in Jesus today and wish to go to heaven and become brides understand? A bride? That sounds nice. Of course, that noun is good.  
But how do we go through the process of righteousness, suffering, sorrow, and misery necessary to establish that noun?  
A price must be paid. One must not become a debtor.  
We must understand the heart of Jesus who carried the cross. Jesus could not lift his face toward heaven, and when he looked at the earth, he wanted to cover his ears because of the cries of betrayal. However, Jesus was in a position where he had to hold onto them as the King of Kings, so he pleaded, “Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do.” He appealed for the historical sins of the Israelite nation to be forgiven, and he forgave the enemies who had caused him grievance, yearning to liberate the lamentation rights that future generations would face.  
In this way, Jesus took responsibility for the path of the cross and steadfastly walked on. Because of this, God was able to establish a historical victory through Jesus' resurrection, to establish a leadership for the times, and to unfold a new historical beginning. Also, because the condition was established that if one follows the resurrected Jesus, one can also be resurrected, the apostles were able to start again. Otherwise, they could not because Satan would accuse them. By establishing even the condition that Jesus forgave the betrayers, the apostles could be re-established based on the standard of having received God's approval and Satan's approval. In this way, we are moving toward reclaiming the sovereignty of heaven.  
You must understand the heart of Jesus who carried the cross. How pitiful a man Jesus was! Can you face Jesus, who has historical value and authority? Do you have the face to look at Jesus of that time? Could you believe in Jesus, who was chased by the Israelite nation that believes in the Old Testament and mocked by the Jews as a madman possessed by Beelzebub?  
How many words must have been said about the young man with unkempt hair who walked around with a widow? What about pouring perfume on his feet and wiping them with his hair? Would you believe in such a Jesus? Even if there are world-renowned theologians who say, “I am the number one bride of the Lord,” would they believe in such a Jesus? They would likely be the first to throw stones. Now that Jesus is recognized as great and his historical value is acknowledged, it is easy to believe.  
The orphan-like Jesus, the wandering Jesus, the one who was labeled a traitor of the nation, the Jesus who carried the cross while shedding pitiful and miserable tears and blood, the wronged and frustrated Jesus, the one who went as a sacrificial offering with unexpressed grievances, who promised to return as long as my blood does not die, as long as my prayer does not die, as long as my wish does not die, as long as my circumstances do not die, as long as my heart does not die, there will be a day of return.  
You should diligently practice your faith and ask Jesus. Jesus had many things he wanted to eat while he was alive. If so, how wonderful would that be? Wouldn't you like to have such power?  
The Reason Jesus Prays at the Right Hand of God  
What kind of prayers did Jesus offer during his preparation period? What kind of prayers did he offer for over 30 years? “God, even if I live like this, do not worry. Living like this is better than living in a palace. Living like this, working hard and laboring, is better than living in luxury in a palace.”  
Even in such a miserable position, Jesus knew historically the will of God who sent him, so he comforted God by saying, “Do not be discouraged. Do not lose heart.”  
For example, if a parent bequeaths all their achievements and possessions to a beloved child, and that child does not keep any for himself but shares everything with his siblings, could the parent call that child and say, “My child, I gave you everything, so why do you live in misery and share everything with your siblings?” and punish him? No, that cannot happen.  
The reason I suffer and live like this is because I know your heart that wants to give and make me the protagonist. Even if I enter a miserable position, when I stand in a good position, I will be gathered before heaven with the opposite value. It is difficult to understand. Do you know what I mean? The lower you go, the greater the value becomes.  
Why did Jesus, who should have eaten well and lived well, suffer and live miserably? It was because all people did not believe in him. For over 30 years, Jesus comforted God while establishing such conditions! Looking at the confused Israelite nation and the forces that were desecrating the temple under Roman oppression, he could not avoid stepping forward, even if it meant preparing for death.  
Thus, for 30 years, with a heart of compassion as the Messiah, he cried out to all people, “Come, follow me!” At the beginning of that path, he resolved hundreds of times that he would fight even if it meant dying.  
However, when all the Jews chased Jesus away, he resolved to fulfill God's will and sought out the lower-class people.  
He sought out people like fishermen, tax collectors, and prostitutes, who were considered the scum of that era. The disciples of Jesus, who came as the King of Kings, were in such a state, so how must have God's heart felt? It was resentful. How much must have Jesus' heart burned with anguish as he gathered those pitiful people and had to command them to manage the world?  
The Jesus who came and went has been working for the providence of salvation for this earth until now. Jesus is said to be praying at the right hand of God, but would he pray if he were comfortable?
Shall we pray when everything is going well? Jesus did not bear fruit. We must understand that Jesus cannot give blessings. 

Why must Jesus return? The purpose of God's restoration history is to restore the entire world. To achieve complete restoration both spiritually and physically, God sent Jesus, and the purpose of Jesus' coming was to fulfill that. However, Jesus left without achieving that purpose. Are we to ask such a Jesus for blessings? I worry that we might lose the blessings we already have. 

Jesus cannot give blessings. He cannot bless the world. Unless Jesus prays and, through God's work, gives blessings, it is uncertain. If Jesus prays and God helps, and if He involves Jesus' disciples to achieve results, then a foundation for global blessings could be laid, but that nation cannot become a blessed nation. Jesus' disciples also did not become blessed apostles. No matter how great an apostle or chief disciple they were, they could not take the position of the bride. An apostle is a servant. They cannot take the position of the bride.

He must compensate for it. That is why He has been praying for 2,000 years. He is a pitiful figure. Who is the most pitiful person in history? It is Jesus.

Because Jesus could not fulfill His wishes, He must start from the position of a failed corpse to restore the global Israel. Since the Israelite nation was completely shattered, He had to restore individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world spiritually, not physically. 

The Israelite nation, which had prepared for 4,000 years to welcome the Messiah, could receive the Messiah both spiritually and physically. We must understand that Jesus is weeping as He looks at the 2,000 years of Christian history. What was the reason for His three prayers in Gethsemane? It was because He knew that if He died on the cross, the descendants of Israel would have to walk the path of the cross. The Israelite nation was to receive salvation both spiritually and physically through Jesus, but since they could not, and since Jesus left with a grievance, He knew that His descendants would also end up like that. Therefore, Jesus, who must atone for the grievances of these descendants, cannot help but come back to this earth. 

On the mountain of Golgotha, God's grievance is bound, and the grievance of the Israelite nation is bound, and the grievances of their descendants and humanity are bound. That is why the path of Golgotha, which stretches for a thousand miles, remains in Christianity. 

You must understand that Christianity is now traversing the path of personal Golgotha, familial Golgotha, and tribal Golgotha to reach the summit of global Golgotha. 

Jesus, who carried the cross, was Jesus who bore historical sorrow, Jesus who bore the sorrow of the age, and Jesus who bore the sorrow of the future. He was Jesus who left with a sense of injustice. The Jesus who should have smashed the cross on the mountain of Golgotha, judged the enemies, and charged forward, died with a sense of injustice. 

That is why Jesus must not die but must live to receive the glory of resurrection. He must come over Golgotha again and take responsibility for leading the Israelite nation. 

Can the bride sleep comfortably while the bridegroom is hungry and weeping? Can the bride eat and sleep comfortably while the bridegroom kneels before God and offers the atoning sacrifice? But what position does Christianity hold today? There should not be a single day of comfort. 

Because Jesus has grievances at the national level, until we surpass that national standard, the history of Christianity must inevitably be miserable. Because when God sent Jesus, it was to resolve the grievance of 4,000 years of history, but since Jesus came and left, God's grievance has increased by the grievance of 2,000 years after Jesus' death. Therefore, today’s Christians must be sadder than Jesus.

The Real Adopted Son and the Fake Adopted Son 

Today, many pastors in established churches say, "Ah, I am a holy servant of God." But can a servant go to heaven? Can a servant's body enter heaven? No, it cannot. Heaven is a place for sons and daughters. 

After receiving the title of a loyal subject, one must enter the position of an adopted son. If one longs to become a direct son and serves faithfully before the Father, they become an adopted son who inherits. If a child of a different lineage enters the position of a direct son and seeks to inherit, saying, "Oh, I will inherit that wealth," then they are not an adopted son. They are a fake adopted son. The real adopted son is one who can say, "Isn't this son the bloodline of the Father?" and when the Father is in pain, they must feel even more pain, and when the Father is sad, they must feel even more sorrow. Since the Father does not have such a son, they must be able to say, "I will be the substitute for that son." 

One must fully possess the qualifications of an adopted son internally before they can inherit and enter the position of a substitute for the son. 

In Romans 8:23, it is written that "we ourselves, who have the first fruits of the Spirit, groan inwardly as we wait eagerly for our adoption as sons." To become an adopted son, Jesus lived as a loyal subject who was faithful to God on the cross and faithful to heaven on earth, so it is the duty of the son to protect Jesus as the Father. Therefore, one must not lose the heart to follow the Father and must walk the path of a loyal subject to become a true adopted son. One cannot fulfill God's restoration providence with the mindset of a thief. This is the understanding of adoption that the teacher knows. 

As a substitute for a direct son, one must struggle and receive God's approval to enter the status of an adopted son and the right of inheritance. We must understand that we are in such a position today. 

Are you still in the position of a servant? If you are in the position of a servant, your faith must exceed that of Abraham. You must suffer more than Jacob did when he went to Haran for 21 years to seize the blessing of the firstborn. Moses suffered more than 120 years—40 years in Pharaoh's palace, 40 years in the Midian wilderness, and 40 years in the journey of returning to Canaan. 

Thus, like Cain and Abel, you must become brothers and say to the Father, "Please acknowledge my elder brother. Please acknowledge my younger brother," so that the Father can say, "Oh, good job." You must establish such a connection on earth to become an adopted son. However, because you have lost the day when you could have such authority as an adopted son, the Christians scattered across the world, who are the first fruits of the Spirit, are longing to become adopted sons. 

Today, we must understand the internal grievances, external grievances, and familial grievances of Jesus. When we look at an individual, we must see them as a historical individual; when we look at a family, we must see it as a historical family; when we look at a tribe, we must see it as a historical tribe; when we look at a nation, we must see it as a historical nation. The one who sought to establish such a religious ideology to create a hopeful nation and a hopeful world is Jesus. We must not think, "Let me live well for myself."

The Significance of the Indemnity Fund

Those who work must engage in activities for several hours each day. In the remaining three years, we must unite and fight harder than last year. Do not worry for yourself; worry for the nation and the world. 

Do not think of what you have as your own. Live all in the name of heaven. 

The indemnity of blood began with Abel, but it must end now. 

We must build an external temple where God can dwell. 

We must support those who are currently working among the 36 families. If we see blessed families starving and do not support them, we will fall under heavenly law. 

Caring for heaven, caring for the earth, and caring for family members is the messianic thought. 

Because of Adam's fall, God's grievance has accumulated, so we must walk the path of indemnifying that grievance from Adam's position. 

Originally, we were to first establish the Day of All Things and then find the Day of Children and the Day of Parents, but the Unification Church has established them in reverse order. The teacher personally established the Day of All Things and the Day of Children, and then on that expectation, established the Day of Parents.
True parents who come with genuine love cannot establish Parents' Day from the perspective of parents without feeling the abandonment from their children. 
These three days have been violated with blood. How will we atone for the sins of killing parents, the sins of killing children, and the sins of abandoning all creation? 
Judas bought a grave for a wanderer with the blood money he received for betraying Jesus. Therefore, we must prepare a place for the saints to stay with the atonement fund. Originally, we should purchase the headquarters. 
What should have taken seven years after liberation has been extended to twenty-one years. 
The atonement fund is the most precious money among all. There must be many anecdotes related to this fund. There must be many miserable events. 
The atonement fund, which represents the sin of Cain who killed Abel, is the blood money of fathers and brothers for the children. From now on, we must gather that fund. 
To celebrate Parents' Day, we must stand in the position of parents, which means we must have children. Therefore, we must evangelize. 

Big achievements require failures
<Summary of the message> When a person starts a task, they make a firm resolution, but if things do not go as planned, that determination gradually fades away. When they fail, they quickly become disappointed, and such people cannot accomplish great things. Those who achieve great things need experiences of failure. 
If one starts with a strength and resources of 10 and fails, they should start the second time with a strength of 100. If they fail again, they should try the third and fourth times with double the strength. There will inevitably be a time when they succeed at least once during ten attempts. 
Most people in the world retreat after failing in the first, second, or third attempts, but our Unification Church youth must resolve to start again even after several failures. 
Hunting wild boars is fun. At first, when people set out towards the mountain ridge, everyone competes to be at the front with all their might, but after crossing several hills, they become exhausted and think, "As long as I can keep going without falling behind, that's enough." However, when they become more out of breath and tired, they start to think, "Maybe I should take a break?" and eventually, they show expressions that suggest they want to stop. It is at this moment that the wild boar escapes. 
When fishing in the sea, at first, it seems like one can catch all the fish in the ocean, but after throwing the net several times with all their spirit and effort, the initial enthusiasm fades, and they become bored. 
Those who hope for good things from the beginning cannot become great people. When good things appear and others are pleased, if one works to find something that only they can have, they will gain great joy. 
This path does not end in 3 or 4 years. Even if it extends to 7 years or 70 years, one must have the determination to continue steadily. The longer the period, the more one must broaden the scope. 
Once a success is achieved, one should steadily work based on that success for the overall success, which will lead to overall victory. If something is successful in a region, do not stop there; the model of that success should be replicated so that the success of districts, regions, and churches can contribute to overall development. 
One should not just rejoice in victories in Suwon. That victory must connect to the victories of districts and churches. If one goes out to the region or district and wins by reflecting on the training in the area, that will lead to the victory of the region. 
I ask you to continue fighting. If national victory does not connect to the victory of your village, you must fight again. Only then can the original purpose be achieved. 
The unfortunate people are our parents and relatives. Knowing this, let us fight until the end. 

Let’s save this nation
<Summary of the message> The Gyeonggi region is the center of the nation, so the church must be large, but it is too small. From now on, we must launch a movement to build a regional headquarters. When members from Seoul come, they should buy at least 10 bricks, and when local members come, they should buy at least 5 bricks. 
The construction cost is about 650,000 won, and if you cover two-thirds of it, I will cover the rest. 
If the Gyeonggi region, which is at the center of the nation, does well, then Seoul will also do well. Our Unification Church was founded with hands and heads. Our work is to atone for the vertical with the horizontal. I also started with nothing, so even if you have nothing, if you unite and believe, God will help you. 
The three-year course may seem tedious, but once it ends, the overall situation changes, and the four-year course will also pass quickly. From now on, the path we take will become easier. 
Currently, in Washington, about a hundred important figures are organized to proclaim our message, and by next year, all 50 states in the U.S. will be active. Foreign members are working hard so that they will not fall behind Korea, so the issue lies with Korea. 
Your pride lies in having worked hard in a place where there is no recognition. Members in America fast for 1 or 2 days each week, and those American members in Seoul fast every Thursday and Friday. 
You may call Japanese people "Yankees," but to me, they are all precious members. 
You should not be someone who is pleased when given and dislikes when asked. 
The headquarters must be built by our hands. 
No matter how hungry you are, you must endure and think of something greater. 
I can be a friend to anyone, regardless of age or gender, but as a Unification Church leader, one must maintain dignity and face. The most comfortable time is when I wear clothes that allow my fingers to come out when I put my hands in my pockets. The higher you go, the harder it becomes. Although we started with nothing, we must move forward with dignity. 
This time, all members nationwide must take the lead in contributing to the atonement fund. We must establish conditions to atone for the tears, sweat, and blood. We must navigate through national adversities based on a national foundation. I hope for the Korean people to be the most unfortunate. This is because our nation must be in the most miserable position to atone without giving. Therefore, we are currently establishing national atonement conditions. 
The path of the cross is the path of suffering. To cross this path of the cross, one must go naked. Jesus also gave away even his last garment. 
The path of Golgotha has both spiritual and physical paths. Since all people are made of spirit and flesh, there are also spiritual and physical paths in Jesus' way to save them. The path of Golgotha must start from the family and extend globally. 
We are currently walking the national Golgotha path. Jesus also walked this path, so as children, we must follow. We must pass on the standard of our spiritual Golgotha to the 30 million people in physical positions. Just as Jesus blessed the Jewish people who disbelieved him and hung him on the cross, you must do the same. 
We must train to be able to take responsibility for the nation in the face of adversity. We must become members who endure until the end. 
God is the richest and happiest being in the universe, yet He is in the most impoverished and unhappy position. Just as God has the most sorrowful heart, so does the teacher. 
When there are opposing groups, do not avoid them, but have something that can subdue them. God raises those who are more devoted in the face of opposition. We must walk the path that good people could not walk. 
We must be those who suffer for the nation and remain devoted until the end. If those responsible in the restoration path cannot fulfill their mission, the will of heaven may be extended for 40 years. 
Whatever you have, it belongs to God, so possess it genuinely. And you must become a righteous person, have a family, and become a new ancestor. The results are sought by heaven in the most arduous places. The value of a son met in a miserable place and the value of a son met in a full place are entirely different in the eyes of the father. 
The one who has clung to history with heartfelt emotion and has struggled to come out is God. The path of restoration is the path stained with blood, sweat, and tears, and it is the path of Golgotha that God seeks and hopes for. Those who walk this path can become global filial sons and daughters and go to that nation. 
God came from a pitiful place, so we must meet God in such a place. The master’s work is to leave what has grown strong in the right place and to weed out what is wrong. As the time approaches, trials also increase proportionately. It cannot be easy to atone for the whole at once. Many seekers have come to the teacher and left their harvest bundles behind. 
In the past, external persecution was severe, so the teacher embraced it internally, but that time has passed, and now it is being pushed hard. This is the teacher's philosophy. 
When Jesus was crucified, think about what the Roman soldiers used to strike him; those who struck him should be punished many times over for their actions. 
The principle of atonement is in three stages: atoning for 3 days, 3 months, and 3 years. Atoning for 40 years in 4 years is indeed a struggle, but this is God's utmost love. 
We must survive in any miserable environment. The teacher makes you suffer to place you in a safe position. Because He is a wise God, even if you die, it is victory, and even if you make you suffer, it is to lead you to victory, so endure until the end. Originally, great leaders tend to make others suffer a lot. To lead the whole world, one must walk the path of global suffering. 
In this four-year course, we aim to create a wind throughout the nation centered on the Gyeonggi region. If 30 million fast one meal a day and save 10 won each, that amounts to 300 million won a day. Korea's annual budget is 60 billion won, and if we collect in this way, Korea can survive without aid. We must not receive foreign aid. 
The teacher had not experienced a day without hunger until he was thirty. This four-year course is to atone for the 4,000 years from Adam to Jesus, and the atonement fund is to repay the blood money of thirty pieces of silver for which Jesus was sold. 
God shed blood to establish the positions of all things, parents, and children, so we must atone for this and establish the temple, the house of life. Only by resolving this can we open the way to welcome God. 
Having built a temple for the body with the blood money of Jesus, we must build a temple for the people with the atonement fund and establish national, state, and global temples. 
If we lay a good foundation for four years, the world will come to us. Therefore, the conclusion is that we must suffer. The higher the mountain, the deeper the valley. There is nothing easy in the world, but the path of restoration becomes easy if only the conditions are set. 
A person must set their goals and pave the way around the age of 30. They must suffer so that they can travel a path that should take ten years in just one year. In such a position, one must never complain. 
The teacher walked out without blaming God even in the bleeding place of prison. You too must go on behalf of God, no matter how difficult the situation may be. In difficult places, call upon God and reflect on what the sorrow of God, the subject of love, is like. 
There will come a time when, according to the teacher's command, both America and Japan will move forward. During this revival period, although you may be eating death, a leader may sometimes sprinkle sand to prevent you from eating even that. You may not know the path of restoration, but the teacher knows it well, which is why he does so. 
There will come a time to teach about such things, but for now, we must first do important work. In the future, people from around the world will come to establish the homeland. We must establish the homeland and create heaven. The reason the teacher travels between the West Sea and East Sea whenever he has time is for this purpose. Until that world comes, endure and suffer and become those who remain until the end. 

About precious things
<Summary of the message> Those who see the teacher for the first time tend to observe him externally, which leads them to become hostile towards him. 
One must be able to kneel and pray for at least three hours or more. 
Everyone in the world desires precious things. Precious things are good, and good things are connected to goodness. If there is a precious item, there must be a precious person to oversee it. 
Young people especially want to claim anything good as their own without exception. However, they must recognize that both precious and undesirable, happy and unhappy things center around themselves. 
Even if the whole is disregarded, if I become a precious being, God will manage everything centered around me. Therefore, conscience desires to become the center that governs the whole. 
To become the center among ten, one must have good relationships with those ten, and when I move, all ten must be able to move as well. To become such a precious being, one must be a central existence that has connections with the past, present, and future. One must be recognized as a central being that the nation acknowledges and has connections with both internally and externally from beginning to end. 
Everyone in the world seeks precious things. If viewed materially, it is gold. No one dislikes this. Moreover, every nation needs this, so it is precious. 
To become a precious person, one must not only be needed in the past but also in the present and future along the path of history. A precious person finds precious things, governs them, and remembers the relationships they have established. 
We must recognize the gratitude we owe to water, air, and sunlight, which absolutely sustain and nurture our lives. All things remain unchanged, but human hearts are always changing. Precious things are absolute beings that transcend time and space. 
Just as there are precious centers among objects, there are also precious centers among humans. If there is a precious and true person through the past, present, and future, then the ideology they speak of is precious. This is because they manage history and pioneer the future. Our sorrow is that we have not found the precious being in the history that seeks a precious being. 
The truer a person is, the harder they are to find, and precious people cannot be obtained through money or treasures. 
If there were precious people that could be bought with money, wars would break out all over the world because of that. However, if a true and precious value exists, the world will unite without force. 
If there is someone who can feel the preciousness of a precious being even in a place of suffering, that person is also precious. 
People, the more precious they are, want to establish a connection with themselves. If that person is a woman, they want to connect as a bride; if a man, as a groom, to make them a person known only to themselves. However, a precious person must repel evil and create a new history, and God must also need them. 
In a place where good and evil coexist, God cannot be present. Until now, the only person who has walked the path where God could be present is Jesus. The one who came to introduce a true person with precious content before heaven is precisely Jesus. Jesus pursued the true human image while being crowded and chased to find the true. 
The central being that humanity desires is also what God desires. The precious center is needed by God and the whole world, but since God values it more, Jesus sought God. Jesus, who came to find true humans, valued God more than the earth, so he lived according to God's will.
. God is the one who is needed before Him, but He is the one who has kept watch until humanity desires Him, and that is the history of the restoration providence. 
Love is absolutely necessary for the true and genuine. The reason why heaven is good is that people embrace and love each other beyond their own ideals. Love is something everyone longs for, and its content is infinite. There is no loss in love, no matter how much one gives. Furthermore, the ultimate thing that humanity needs is love. No matter how strong the sunlight is, it cannot turn evil into good, but love can certainly do that. 
In the path of restoration, one must do what can ultimately be beneficial, even if it incurs some loss along the way. Show interest in what you need. Everything in the world is good material that can shape your character. All of creation was needed by God. 
The most precious thing that people seek is love. Humans live seeking precious things, precious people, and precious love. God is the center of love that has no beginning or end, and He governs heaven and earth eternally. The center of all precious creation is humanity, and the center of precious love is God. 
To find people, God has sacrificed material and humanity to seek love. Love is the oneness of two! This is what God, who has come to us, wishes to give to humanity. In a place where there is no bond formed by love, people scatter, but when centered on love, they gather. 
God has come to give humanity the most precious thing until today. Jesus, as the prince sent by God, is called the bridegroom of humanity, but has today’s Christianity truly understood what this bridegroom desires and dislikes? 
God wishes to give all of creation to His children, even Himself. The one who has formed a bond with such a God is the Lord, and those who are in harmony with such a Lord have everything that belongs to the Lord as their own. 
Since God is the one who wishes to give the most precious things, let us become people who can appreciate the gifts we have received.

The Universe Does Not Rest
<Summary of the Message> Until now, it has been a history of consumption for the sake of giving. However, from now on, it will be a history of gathering and flourishing. 
Today, the ritual of subjugating the substantial Satan, which will take place in three stages, signifies establishing the sovereignty of goodness with the authority of the original world and ruling centered on heart. Now, we must establish the foundation where God can directly govern the created world by setting up the parents who fulfill the mission of the father and mother. 
To establish this foundation, God has walked the path of labor and the path of the cross. Now, God will gather what has been given and establish the public merit of righteousness to transition into a new era. 
Until now, the Holy Spirit has been in the position of fallen humanity to restore the Holy Spirit era, but from now on, the Holy Spirit must be able to directly judge injustice. Until now, wrongs have been neglected, but from now on, we must mobilize the good spiritual world to demand responsibility. 
We have entered a new era where we must directly welcome the Father. From now on, we must act by receiving the Father’s commands directly. 
Until now, we have been engaged in work to make indemnity, but from now on, we must work to make indemnity happen. Therefore, you must stand in the position of the Holy Spirit. You must also stand as a public entity representing the whole, not as an individual. Personal feelings or grievances should not hinder the public righteousness. 
Ignore the personal and stand in the public position. Everyone must stand in the position of children centered on the Father. If you live like this, God will work anew. If there are those who have not fulfilled their responsibilities, they will be held accountable. 
Restoration is centered on the father-son relationship, so no matter how difficult the circumstances, if you live centered on God, you can gather all grace and subjugate all spirits. From now on, all spirits will come toward this place. Therefore, you must act on behalf of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. 
You must dedicate everything to meet God’s requirements. You must also absolutely comply with public commands. Even if that command is wrong, obedience will turn it into a blessing. 
From now on, you must lead a new life before God. Even if the teacher does not speak, you have the responsibility to guide. You must realize all the grace given by God. 
This ritual is one that reunites what has been divided in spirit. Your concern for the purpose must be greater than for yourself. Until now, it has been the labor of indemnity, but from now on, it will be the labor to establish your own merit before God. 
Until now, the Holy Spirit has worked indirectly, but from now on, God will work directly. You must also work on behalf of the teacher. The second ritual held at noon will be one that does not tolerate injustice and reunites the divided heaven and earth, and also mobilizes the spiritual world to develop a new fight based on new commands, thus clearing the substantial Satan from the earth. 
<Prayer> Everything present here symbolizes light, glory, and holiness, and flowers signify all fruits. Please establish a new law centered on parents. Amen. 
<Exhortation> Do not leave your own children to others. If parents are weak and must leave their children to someone else, they should leave them to someone who will love them like their own firstborn. Raising a child should be done with the thought of raising them for the nation and the world. 
The teacher’s children should be raised by devoted parents. 
People must bear the three-fold responsibility toward family, nation, and heaven. You must understand that your own well-being is for the betterment of all people. 
Since leaving good things on earth is the history of the restoration providence, if parents stand in a good position, God will give them children who resemble their good traits. A wife must diligently cook and offer food for her husband. 
Do you have something to give to others? You must give the best of what you have. That is giving life, which means giving the Word. 
Korea must give the best to the world. 
In the future, blessed families must be judged by the people of the world. They must receive recognition from all the spirits scattered around. When you go toward the center, there may be no words, but if you want to stand directly at the center, you must receive recognition from all sides. In the future, many spiritual beings will stand before the purpose. 
We must know whether we have lived for the purpose or have lived by the purpose. There are those who observe what will happen to those who have received blessings and those who have not. When a baby calls out "Daddy," God does not hear it as just one baby’s voice but as the voice of all babies. 
God gives grace after trials. Every time the teacher sees someone with a clever head, he feels sorrow for how little has been accomplished by that age. If the Father sheds tears ten times, we should shed tears at least once. The blood, sweat, and tears shed in the presence of the Father are different from the blood, sweat, and tears shed historically. Let us meet the Father who has come to this nation and embrace Him, shedding tears. 
There are those who disrupt the whole because of a single day’s mood. 
Since God created the environment before making Adam and Eve, we must first lead the environment to peace. If we harbor sadness in our hearts, it will become a sickness. We must cast away this sadness. To do so, we must pray or endure hardships. The reward will be determined by how much we have suffered and how much we have lived for others. Since Jesus bore wounds for all people, it is glorious if we have left any marks on our bodies for our nation. 
God blesses such people. 
2nd Ritual (Noon) 
<Summary of the Message> If we convey this message with the conviction that injustice cannot stand before the Word, fear will come to the world of Satan through this message. From now on, a history of taking away the birthright will take place centered on the Word. As we convey the Word, the spiritual beings will also cooperate. 
The ritual performed in the morning was to establish the conditions for heart judgment, and the ritual performed at noon is to establish the conditions to unite the divided heaven and earth before God and the heavens centered on the Word. Until now, this Word has faced slander from the world, but that will not be the case from now on. From now on, it will spread widely as we act.

<Summary of the Message> Following the first and second rituals, this ritual establishes the conditions for personality judgment. The ritual concerning the nation (Republic of Korea) is the last one. It is not necessary to perform a ritual for the world. The suffering of the nation and the church becomes the standard for subjugating the substantial Satan. 
Let us not deceive our conscience. This will be recorded in heaven. 
What has been burned in the water of the fountain of life is akin to Moses burning the idol and eating it; it is burning and consuming Satan. If you continue to advance with the joy of victory, it will remain as your own achievement. Now that you have established these conditions, have confidence that you can subjugate Satan.
