Let Us Raise the Wind of Hope
<Summary of the Message> There are various winds blowing in the world, and in Korea, there is a wind of despair. So what kind of wind should the Unification Church raise? 
We must raise a wind that takes responsibility for all the cries of despair, hunger, and difficulty. 
We are currently in the 7-year course, having passed the 3-year course and are now unraveling the threads of the 4-year course. We have always left behind unique ideologies and actions, and we are still fighting with such a purpose. 
The weak are absorbed by the strong; this is the principle of power. In light of this principle, our Unification Church must raise strength for this nation and people. The Unification Church has the responsibility to support the weary and lift up those who have fallen. 
The world and the nation are in a state of confusion. At this time, even those who entered the Unification Church first are also in a state of confusion, and we must again raise the tide of strength. 
Your steps and gazes must not be lifeless. If we seriously consider that what we are doing is what God desires, what the spirits desire, and what all our members desire, we will surely achieve great results. 
June 10, 1964 (Wednesday) Afternoon, Daegu Church. 
* This message has been organized from what was published in <Gyeonggi Front> No. 10, with the title added by the editor.
We must fight until the end. 
Today, our numbers are small, but we have many spirits behind us, and we know that there are brothers preparing abroad. Let us not forget that we are the soldiers of the Unification Church marching forward. 
The Unification Church may be quantitatively at a disadvantage, but we must stand in absolute superiority qualitatively. When we give our all in loyalty and sincerity, it will bear fruit as good results. 
Though our numbers are few, if we are more loyal to God than the current Christians, the fate of Christianity will be through us. 
The more we strive for God's will and loyalty, the more we hasten the destruction of the sinful world and are given another responsibility to fulfill. 
Whether we see results or not, if we are loyal and sincere, the outcome will manifest as good fruit. 
We must be like cannonballs, moving straight towards our purpose, certain to explode. 
On the last day of the lunar month of April (June 9), the teacher went through a three-part battle (the ceremony of subjugating the substantial Satan) with the members. 
We must raise the vitality of hope and ideology to give a great shock to this nation, which is on the path of death. 
We must create a wind that says there is nothing beyond the gatherings, words, and people of the Unification Church. 
Although the Unification Church faces external conditions such as hunger and nakedness, we must not lose our place and center, no matter how difficult the conditions are. 
We must become people who connect the world's pain and worries with our own worries and pain. 

Fulfill the duty of loyalty before God 
<Summary of the Words> When the teacher was laboring in Hungnam prison, ten people had to bind a thousand bags of fertilizer within eight hours a day. Achieving that goal was extremely difficult, but knowing that God was doing even harder work than I was, I was able to overcome it. Others were exhausted thinking about food because they were hungry. However, those who found joy in working amidst such circumstances do not feel the hardship. 
Even though the teacher was in prison for nearly three years, he only suffered from fever once and did not know any other illness. However, no matter how much he was in pain, he worked without taking medicine, even fasting. At that time, he suffered from fever for twelve days (24 days) but worked without resting at all. 
Those who seek to avoid hard work cannot endure it. One must be able to overcome difficulties and sustain themselves for six months to a year or more. 
Even if I do not speak, comrades who can go for me must appear and be found. In Hungnam prison, the teacher did not say a word, but the descendants of good ancestors came to him. The teacher took care of those who came with all his strength and sincerity. He once saw them suffering with their fingers bleeding while binding fertilizer bags, so he untied a rope to make thimbles and distributed them to them. If there are more than twelve comrades who can go with him to the ends of hell, he will not fall. 
When walking the path of indemnity, one must go independently. Therefore, one must not rely on others when establishing conditions for indemnity, nor should one do anything that can be slandered by everyone. 
One must know how to protect oneself even in the most difficult positions. In any position, one must concentrate their mental strength and not yield. The teacher, even in the difficult position of Hungnam prison, would wash his body with a wet towel every morning and night. Although it was hard to find water, he would somehow manage to get it during the day to wash his body. If caught, it would be a big deal, but he continued without missing a day. Within the established rules, one must find their own way to survive. If you fall behind in work, you lose. 
The hardest work in Hungnam prison was continuously filling fertilizer for eight hours and weighing fertilizer bags. This was something everyone disliked, but the teacher took it upon himself and accomplished it. 
Principles must not be limited by time and space. Obedience must be done with a joyful heart. The path of restoration is the path of indemnifying oneself. 
The process of resurrection is like a snake shedding its skin as it passes through a rock crevice. One must establish principled standards and compare them to avoid breaking. This is the principle. 
When engaging in public work, one must be serious. The teacher does not want you to be looked down upon when you go out to the regions. You must stand in a position to judge them. The teacher could turn the world around overnight with the strategy of subjugating Satan, but in the position of teaching good disciples, one cannot use the same strategy as when subjugating enemies. 
Do not receive wages for a day's work; think of it as saving for humanity. How joyful that is! 
God does not teach you when you pray, if knowing is worse than not knowing. 
Walk the rainy streets with the heart of a loser. You must also be able to feel the heart of a loser. 
Is there anyone who does not love their own children? Feel the heart of the teacher who left his family and headed toward North Korea. Everyone must overcome such critical moments. If you do not embrace all people, they will not clean the nest of my love for you. 
God is looking for soldiers who can capture the enemy even without your intervention. Even if you go to a small village, there must be comrades who will cooperate on their own. Since the teacher has walked this path until now, you must also walk such a path. 
The friendship of a man who cries wanting to see another man remains as love even in heaven. You must become someone who can transcend eating, sleeping, and seeing what you want. 
Suffering is wonderful. Therefore, we must establish a tradition that future generations can be proud of for thousands of years. 
The word father is a fearful word. Without truth, one cannot feed and raise their children. One must feed their children with the merits of blood and goodness. When they eat what is wrong, they must guide them with tears and bless them; that is what a parent is. Therefore, parents do not rely on their children. 
The money I use must be known by heaven and earth. 
If there is a way to indemnify the conditions of 6,000 years of restoration history all at once without losing my life, 
I must say, "Please give it to me!" 
Do not deceive your conscience, knowing that the time of judgment is approaching. 
Do not pass the conditions of indemnity to the next generation; establish them in your own generation. Shed holy blood, tears, and sweat, and endure suffering upon suffering. Indemnity does not just happen. 
A true leader who can lead a thousand must be able to shed tears more than a thousand times, and to lead thirty million, must be able to shed thirty million tears. 
There may come a time when you cannot lift your head before God. Strive not to let that happen. You must pave the way for this nation. With the ideology of the teacher, with the body of the teacher, let us shed tears for thirty million and pave the way. 
Our ideology is to fight with our lives to achieve that and to feel joy in the place of suffering. 
If one cannot fulfill their responsibilities, they must sleep without stretching their legs. 
One who cannot fulfill their responsibilities and enters their home will be too embarrassed to look at the eaves. Only such a person can become a true leader. 
We have a path to walk and a responsibility to fight. We must become people who dedicate ourselves fully to our entrusted tasks. Be the kind of people who can run to see your family. 
The only way to conquer God is through loyalty, and the only way to conquer parents is through filial piety. Therefore, you must fulfill the duty of loyalty and filial piety before God. 
Now is the time to prepare and act. Please do not tire, do not fall, and do not die; survive. Now, whether you die or live, it is victory. Once we pass 1967, the spirit world will be mobilized. 
If America does not aid Korea, it will perish. Since the Kennedy administration cannot do this, God is raising the members of the Unification Church to do it. 
The teacher plans to create a resort for neurotic patients worldwide. Wouldn't that still lead to evangelism? 
From 1960 to 1967 is a period of great tribulation globally. 
Our hope is to have good ancestors, to become good ancestors, and to create good ancestors. Therefore, we must go out vigorously and fight. 

Our stage 
<Summary of the Words> The teacher is planning strategies on how to enter national institutions to give principle lectures to save this country. 
Let us save this country with the results of our activities. We must move the local leaders, such as the county head and the village chief. And this time, the Daegu Church must establish a foundation to move on its own. Focus on evangelizing those who can be immediately used for the purpose. 
While traveling back and forth, pray, "Father! Please allow me to meet someone to evangelize." Let each person achieve their responsibility in their respective districts through their efforts. 
We have learned a philosophy that enjoys being right. To save this fallen world, we must take a leap of adventure. If we want to become historical ancestors, we must achieve something historical and establish a tradition. 
Marriage is not for oneself. If you marry centered around yourself and give birth to children like a fool, your family will perish. Living a fun life through such a marriage is merely a dream. The future is at stake. 
One must enable the nation to move based on the historical foundation they have moved. 
Even when they settle a little, worldly people want to build fences. But you must expand the settled ground even further. 
Now everyone is needed. It is the era of building houses. Start by building the regional headquarters and then the district headquarters. 
When laying the cornerstone, it must be placed so that even if you stack ten layers or a hundred layers on top, it does not budge. The issue is how to build the first seven-year course. 
To follow the Unification ideology, one must go through ten years. For seven years, one must move under orders, and for three years, one must move independently. 
We grow by turning insults into fertilizer. Having received much insult in a place where we would not be insulted, we think we can do even greater things. This is a grand strategy. 
If the rumor spreads that "if you meet the Unification Church group with eyes properly set, you cannot help but attend the meeting," then the thirty million people of this nation will be evangelized in a day. During this period, receive much insult. Even if fifty people insult you, if one hundred fifty praise you, that is enough. 
Concentrate your interest on everything and take action. First, seek methods. 
Study human philosophy. A leader must possess something stronger and tougher than anyone else. One must be able to manage many people and many events to become a broad-minded leader. Wherever you go, meet many people and study them. 
You must be able to shout, "Who will conquer my thoughts and ideas?" 
Do not be a spectator; become an actual performer. 
In the busy times, when will you prepare? Young people must have a fast tempo. Know that this is a period for you to train and act for yourselves, and work hard. You must be thorough in preparation for the descendants of a hundred years later who will think of today's work. 
You will be buried in the place you are assigned. You will become the first to be buried centered around the heavenly ideology. Thinking like this is serious. 
Become a founder. Reconstruction is about gathering existing materials, but founding is about creating new materials. Our ideology is founding. 
"Founding comrades, they are fearsome people." Become people like explosives. 
Falsehood is created from the feet, while truth is created from the head. 
Everywhere we move, we must always add value to others. 
Even among those moving on the same stage, the one who can manage the work becomes the master. 
Even if you suffer humiliation for a day, if it allows you to embrace thirty million in ten years, it is absolutely not a shameful thing. 
The teacher fought and won even in prison. Those who fight with patience can win anywhere and will relatively gain comrades. In prison, it has been proven through action rather than words. If you do so, people will follow without direct words. 
Before a complete subject, an object must always appear. This is the truth. 
Learn everywhere. Such a person receives revelations even from the footsteps of a passing beggar or the cries of birds. If you do not think and care, you cannot establish a relationship with good things. Think and care to establish a relationship with good things. 
The teacher visited all the temples across the country for three years and met the leaders there to sense the fate of Buddhism. 
The glory of victory in battle belongs to the descendants of those who remain until the end. 
Communism is already a setting sun. Islam and Christianity are extremes. 
At this point, I am pushing you toward a focal point in the world. That path is not one to be explained as you go. It can only be explained after you have results. 
Heavenly work is like that. 
You must have a great interest in the teacher and establish a relationship with the stage the teacher is moving toward. The teacher is pushing you to establish relationships with those who do not have interest in him. 
Our country is surrounded by the sea on three sides, so we must pay great attention to the sea. 
You are the encyclopedia and living statue of the seven-year course. You will be dispatched abroad as exemplary figures. 
Study. The time will come when you will be thrust into the stage of ability. The teacher is also studying now. 
Suffer. No matter how difficult things get, endure until the end in that place. After it passes, something will remain. Let us establish this tradition. 

About the Indemnity Fund 
<Summary of the Words> Indemnity is absolutely necessary to go through the process of restoration. Indemnity requires sacrifice. Throughout the history of restoration, many people have been sacrificed. Behind indemnity, there has been sacrifice centered on blood. 
To indemnify the blood that good people have shed, there are two methods: to shed good blood to indemnify the whole or to shed evil blood to indemnify the whole. God has gone through this process to establish all things, find children, and even reach the position of parents. 
Jesus wanted to adopt the Israelite nation and inherit to the direct line, but they could not believe and ended up separating. With the death of Jesus, the path for the Israelite nation to become adopted ended. However, through Jesus bearing the cross, those who believe in the Lord can enter the register of adoption and reach paradise. Therefore, by welcoming the Lord who comes upon this foundation of adoption and submitting to Abel as a Cain-like son before God, restoration occurs. We must establish the path of indemnity on this course. 
The purpose of restoration is to become true children and to have true parents. Just as God blessed after Adam and Eve, the history of restoring all things is also accomplished through true subjectivity.
The reason this world has not come before God is because the True Parents shed blood. To restore this, the Lord who comes must establish the Day of Parents, the Day of Children, and the Day of All Things. Therefore, we have sought the holy sites centered on the Day of All Things. Only by indemnifying the blood that was shed can we resolve the grievances of the whole. The sin of killing the parents is difficult to wash away. We must establish the conditions that can cleanse this, so that heaven and earth can return as one.

Because Jesus was killed while walking the path of vertical historical indemnity, for the past 2,000 years on earth, we have been going through the horizontal path of indemnity. We must inherit the price of all the blood shed horizontally through the Lord who is coming. This period is the four-year period we are in now. 

Until the Lord who is coming becomes the True Parent, He has passed through the position of a servant, then a stepchild, and then the position of a direct child. Because Christians have not accepted the Lord who is coming as their own, He has started from the most miserable position. Thus, the Lord who is coming seeks the form of the 12 disciples in prison, and after establishing a foundation to achieve victory and create heaven, He develops from there. Even in prison, He must break through the depths of hell and go through a national path centered on Christianity.

We have come this far through such a path. We have developed from a place without freedom. After enduring countless hardships, we have paved the way for the position of a stepchild, a child, and a parent. By paving this path, we have established the principle of the cross.

The Lord who is coming has fulfilled the conditions of indemnity in history and the purpose of shedding blood. Therefore, He has resolved the grievances of heaven and earth. However, since the children have not resolved their grievances, the condition to resolve this is the indemnity fund. The parents have triumphed, but since the children have been invaded by Satan, we must resolve the grievances of having sold the parents on the foundation of the victorious parents. Only by preparing the indemnity fund will there be a leap in development. No matter how much the children welcome the parents and possess heaven and earth, they cannot resolve the grievances of the blood shed by the True Parents.

Today's Christianity is a mature tree, and the Lord who is coming appears as the one who has the mission of completion. Democracy must submit to Christianity, and Christianity must submit to the Lord who is coming. We must receive indemnity greater than the sin of killing the parents. This is not something you can do; it can only be done by the command of the victorious Lord.

We must resolve the grievances of heaven and earth and tear down the walls that are blocking this land. Thus, we must create a headquarters centered on the righteous people who have paved the way of virtue until now. This indemnity fund is for global indemnity. The indemnity fund must be given with blood, sweat, and sincerity. You should not take out what you have saved in the bank.

This recommendation is the last one before the members of the Unification Church. The cross before us is now the last one. The past environment of persecution and tribulation has passed, so now we are moving toward a position of loyal subjects and faithful subjects that can be recognized before God. We are also transitioning to a foundation of loyalty and filial piety recognized by heaven and earth in this era. Therefore, those who are loyal to heaven and earth at this time are in a position to have triumphed through two eras and can judge evil.

The teacher's hope was the indemnity fund. We must repay the price of the blood that killed the True Parents. With this offering, we must prepare a sanctuary, that is, a place of atonement, where those wandering in this world can come and find rest.

While the national issue is significant, repay this indemnity fund with sincerity during this four-year period. The path you are taking in the three-year and four-year periods is the time to repay the price of the True Parents' blood. The indemnity fund must be given with sincerity, without eating or wearing, and must be given directly by oneself without going through someone else's hands. By establishing this indemnity fund as a tradition, all our descendants must also cross this hill. When this is accomplished, the fortune of the nation will change. Although it may not be visible on the surface, there is a well bubbling deep within, and if a hole is made, it can explode with power. We must be able to offer sacrifices as priests and ministers who perform this sacred offering without others knowing.

Until now, we could be forgiven for not knowing, but there is no forgiveness in the position of knowing. However, since we are still ignorant, there is a path of forgiveness. That is why we are told to be gentle and humble.

Now is the night period, so nothing is visible. But when the sun rises, everything will be seen. We must successfully pass this crucial point of the four-year period.

The great gathering is one condition to successfully pass the indemnity period. The local areas are conducting activities centered on you, and the headquarters is conducting activities centered on the teacher. Therefore, this time you must do your utmost in loyalty.

Even if the members of the Unification Church cannot do anything else, they must know the value of indemnity and contribute to the indemnity fund. The reason we do not give this command to foreign members is that Korea has not yet ended.

On the coldest day, if you take a cold water bath and put in your sincerity, the indemnity will be great. Do what everyone dislikes and receive recognition. Let us be those who voluntarily do what others do not. At that time, we can overcome the history of salvation without bearing the cross of Jesus.

**Our Attitude Towards Nature and the Nation**

<Summary of the Words> When the teacher was young, he had a deep interest in beautiful birds. He would spend days searching to find out what the bird eats, where it builds its nest, and where it lays its eggs. He also collected hundreds of types of grass to study which ones are poisonous and which ones are medicinal, and to understand their structures.

A person who knows the value of nature
Every time the teacher looked at nature, he deeply pondered how God created all these things. When he looked at acorn trees or various leaves, he thought about how they were made, and everything seemed endlessly mysterious.

Can you create even a single stone?
The teacher has caught countless snakes.

We must have a great interest in everything. Only after knowing the content about it can we truly dominate it. Just knowing the inherent value of nature brings us indescribable blessings. 

On June 20, 1964 (Saturday), at Donggureung (located in Guri-eup, Namyangju-si, Gyeonggi-do).
* This message has been compiled from <Seonghwa> No. 38 (published on August 1, 1964).

When that happens, we will ultimately realize that nature was created around me. However, people do not know this fact. They cannot see nature.

Nature is truly mysterious. If we know this, even the sound of the wind sounds like wonderful music. And it greatly helps our faith life.

Nature is the closest thing to our bodies. Therefore, we must fulfill the wishes of nature that is groaning.

Only those who can love the mountains can revere what is high. In that sense, Confucius, Buddha, and Jesus were all people who loved the mountains.

When the teacher visits scenic spots, he looks at how much value they have centered on heaven's fortune. And he connects that to heaven's fortune. Therefore, in the early days of the Unification Church, he often traveled through the mountains.

By looking at a country's mountains, land, and water, one can understand the national character of that country. The water of our country is precious wherever you go.

We must first achieve the restoration of nature. Before going abroad, we must deeply love the nature of our own country.

A person who can love the land where they were born can also love their own body. And a person who loves their body is one who loves their heart, and a person who loves their heart is one who loves God. Therefore, such a person will not perish. Moreover, such a person cannot be struck by heaven. We must love the land where we were born even more than Niagara Falls. We must understand how many people nature has comforted in God's providential path.

Today, the situation in our country is filled with anxiety. Everyone dislikes this environment. Therefore, a great resolution is needed now.

We are the ones who must create a new world. The older generation has already passed. And the era of children has not yet come, so now is the era of youth. At this point, the youth must be concerned about the situation of our country.

When looking at fallen humans from God's perspective today, we must either completely eliminate them or immerse them in water and recreate them. If left as they are, nothing will happen. In any case, it must come to an end. However, God is a God of love. God cannot kill the humans He created as His children. Therefore, recreation must happen. In terms of surgery, God is in the position of a surgeon.

A person who can bear the responsibility of the nation
Now there is a country that has become like a patient who has lost consciousness and collapsed due to a festering sore, and that country is Korea. We Koreans often say we want to die more than three times a day. Such words are wrong. Words arise from the heart. Korea must undergo surgery from God.

In the history of providence, the foundation of revolution has been laid from a place of suffering. If tears do not suffice, then sweat must be shed, and if sweat does not suffice, then blood must be shed. Tears, sweat, and blood—that was the order of revolution.

In any era of revolution, the upper class seeks refuge while the lower class tries to establish their own. If there are young people trying to establish something here, that country will prosper.

In cases where an individual has fallen into ruin, it takes more than three generations to correct it. Therefore, it will take decades to correct a nation.

Only those who possess the mindset of enduring more suffering can lead this country.

We need someone who can bring forth something new. That is why God loves those who struggle to hold onto those who are not tainted by evil. There must be parents who can nurture from infancy with sincerity. Now we need loyal subjects who care for the young. The Unification Church has been leading you to create such people.

We must look toward the middle and know the lower, and receive recognition from them. The suffering of blessed families also has meaning in this regard.

If you feel pity for your own child, you must also recognize that the children of 30 million are equally pitiable. If that happens, his child will not perish.

Because God has seen the depths of the earth, the history of restoration has occurred. The fortunes of heaven and earth rise and fall. Then they rebound and leap even higher.

One-third of humanity governs this world. High pressure naturally moves toward low pressure, and now our country is in a low-pressure position. Therefore, we must support Korea from all sides. Korea is a place that needs help. Now is the time when other countries must sacrifice lives beyond mere offerings for this nation, but since no such countries exist, our nation must accomplish this.

We must instill thoughts and ideologies in this nation and also instill the power to practice them. We must do this with the heart of a parent raising a child. Therefore, we must receive the recognition of parents, the acknowledgment of siblings, and the approval of children. Giving must be done with tears, blood, and sweat.

If the entire nation cannot take responsibility, then a small group must do so. If this small group fulfills its responsibility, the entire nation will be blessed. When the entire nation repents for the past they could not take responsibility for, they will exalt that small group.

To accomplish anything great, the foundation must be solid. What attitude should our young people take today? Will you be the locomotive or the passenger car? Of course, you must be the locomotive. However, we are currently in a position where we are attached to the back of the passenger car, rolling the wheels backward while trying to follow along.

If we lack strength, we must still roll the empty wheels and cross this hill. We must pull the locomotive.

We must become a unified group with strength. The impulse to move must be 100 percent ingrained in us. Above all, you need the dynamic impulse to push against strength.

What young people must know above all is the question of where I am going from where I am. I must know what attitude is needed for me to live today.

Now is a comfortable time for those who have not yet achieved success.

Whatever it may be, if the motivation is derailed from the beginning, the process and result cannot be right. Both cause and effect must be good. No matter how well a grass sprout has grown, if it does not bear fruit in the fall, it is worse than a frail sprout that has borne fruit.

If there is a 70-year-old man walking here, he has walked a life path in a certain direction from childhood to now at 70 years old. Likewise, we must also be bound to a certain place. We must continue until we find individuals, families, nations, and the world centered on God. The teacher is still walking with that pure heart and attitude he had when he faced God in his youth. That is something that will never change.

Maintain three points
We must be able to maintain a straight line with God, God's purpose, and my purpose at three points. Thus, we must become a drill that pierces through the world of evil that harms the world.

There is no room for compromise on the path of restoration. When we came into this world, we came alone, but we cannot leave alone. We must take many people with us. Humans cannot live apart from society. The reason Jesus went to find His betraying disciples is rooted in this. We must understand the sorrow of Jesus, who could only take one robber with Him. Knowing this situation, we must organize ourselves.

We are moving forward from myself to the 3 billion people of all humanity. When we know that 30 million people leave without salvation in a year, we cannot remain still. If we can shorten what could take a hundred years to save into ten years, we will save many dying people.

We must transcend class. Thus, we must establish conditions for indemnity. All people are equal. If you discriminate against others, at some point, you will also be discriminated against. If you give your hard-earned money to the people of that country while starving yourself, those people will look up to you.

All humanity is material for the restoration of Adam. Therefore, the 6,000 years of history can be said to be the history of the restoration of Adam. To achieve this purpose, we must transcend bloodlines.

This year and next year are crucial. Now that the three-year period is over, the teacher will rest during the remaining four-year period.

Now is the time for ancestors to cooperate for the restoration of this nation. When searching for the nation, we must search broadly, but to do that, I must first become one with God and find society. It is not that we find society first and then God. After that, we must find the nation.

We must always grasp the trends of this society well and navigate toward our purpose.
We must go through this. The greater the mission, the greater the indemnity.  
Individuals must sacrifice for the church, the church for the nation, and the nation for the world. One must be able to sacrifice the small for the sake of the great. There may be individuals who are called to sacrifice for their families or tribes. There may also be families, tribes, or nations that exist for this purpose. Without doing so, one cannot establish a path to victory in world history.  
To establish the expectation of familial victory, indemnity must also be established at the familial level. Noah built the ark for 120 years amidst opposition from the world, and Jacob was deceived by Laban ten times before he reclaimed what was his. Jesus also became the Messiah only after being beaten in the world of Satan. However, if he had faced that with the nation, he would not have died. In this way, those whom heaven has established must first be struck by Satan.  
Our Unification Church also has a historical mission, and thus must stand in a position of being overwhelmed. The historical misery must be represented personally and familially within the Unification Church. When the nation that opposed the Unification Church stands in a position of suffering, it must know that the time has come.

110   Be Victorious  
The crisis lasts until the lunar August. The question is how to establish a loyal soldier who will not tire in this fight. A military force is needed for battle. We must stand in a position of victory personally, tribally, and nationally at once. We must become ourselves and our nation that can heed heaven’s command. To become a loyal soldier, one must go through a miserable path. If this does not happen, this nation will also be struck. At that time, indemnity must be reapplied.  
The purpose of the offering is to find the substance, and the substance is to host God. Now is the time when people are needed, so we must abandon our greed for material things. If America prioritizes money and material, it will perish. Therefore, we must give our beloved sons and daughters to the world.  
In the future, the time will come when people will no longer be centered, and the time will come when ideologies will be centered, and even that time will pass, and the time will come when heaven will be centered.  
We must first be struck from heaven’s side. Only after being struck to the end can we defeat Satan. Therefore, the Unification Church must voluntarily and without complaint endure first. By doing so, the time will come when all humanity will be centered on God.  
We must accept Cain from an Abel-like position and treat him with love.  
The teacher prays for Japan, America, and England.

If our side’s army wins during the expedition, that person also becomes a victorious soldier. This is the meaning behind mobilizing the members.  
20) Our Mission is Great  
<Summary of the Message> When we reflect on the history of the chosen people, we know that the ancestors of faith repeatedly made mistakes at the end of their journeys. Such events have occurred throughout the history of the entire Israelite nation, from the family of Adam to the families of Noah and Abraham, and have continued in the historical process up to the present day after Jesus came and went.  
Indemnity conditions proportional to the mission  
People unanimously say that this time is the last days. In these last days, if God is to judge humanity and fulfill His will on this earth, He will undoubtedly first choose and establish a certain group. Then He will appoint a leader who can guide that chosen group. We cannot assert that those leaders will not make mistakes and repeat the historical errors of the past.  
Therefore, the more we understand the mistakes of our ancestors, the more we must feel and realize how great our responsibility is today.  
Today, the Unification Church has emerged before the Korean church community, and a new ideology of unification has appeared before many nations, which will become a significant issue in the future. Our Unification Church has come bearing a mission of the times. And we have come to take responsibility for the part of the mission that God desires in this end time. You must also feel and realize this for yourselves.  
Responsibility lies with each of you, and it also lies with the entire Unification Church. You must understand that the mission of the members of the Unification Church is to take on the responsibilities that this nation has failed to fulfill by combining individual responsibility and collective responsibility.  
If this mission is a historical mission presented by heaven for this nation and for the 3 billion people of humanity, we have a significant duty to fulfill before the 3 billion people. To bear this responsibility and for the individual and the entire church to unite in carrying this out on the national and global stage, we cannot walk a path of ease. In the providence of restoration, there are always indemnity conditions that must be met in proportion to the process of victory for any individual. If the scope is small, there are indemnity conditions proportional to that small thing, and if the scope is large, there are indemnity conditions proportional to that large thing.  
In this historic end time, to fulfill the mission entrusted to us, we must also bear the indemnity conditions proportional to our mission. The greater the mission, the wider the scope, the more we must fulfill the corresponding indemnity conditions. This is the responsibility and mission that you and the Unification organization must earnestly realize today.  
The purpose of finding individuals is to establish the church, the purpose of establishing the church is to establish the nation, the purpose of establishing the nation is to establish the world, and the purpose of restoring the world is to establish heaven and earth. Thus, sacrificing the small to build the greater is the overall view of the history of restoration that we know well.  
It is essential to complete the indemnity conditions for the whole from the individual standard, as well as to present indemnity conditions for the family, tribe, nation, and even the world, and to confront Satan with the stakes of victory or defeat. Therefore, whether it is an individual, family, tribe, nation, or world, we must establish the final indemnity conditions until there are no further conditions that Satan can present. This is the responsibility and mission that the warriors of unification must bear.  
Indemnity offerings necessary in the path of restoration history  
Now God has allowed us to raise a new flag before the 3 billion people of humanity and to begin the march of a new history. Although the outward appearance of the church is humble, the connections behind it reach back to the ideal realm before creation. Today, we must recognize that the limited environment of unification that has appeared here is connected to the historical ties of the entire world on our shoulders.  
Here, you must be victorious. Our church must be victorious. We must pave the way to present a new ideology before all of humanity and achieve victory.  
The more you resolve to do this, the more you must understand that the corresponding sacrifices and indemnity conditions will follow.  
At any time, God may call you, that is, any member of the Unification Church, and command you to fulfill your individual responsibility and become an offering of indemnity representing your family, or He may call an individual to present the victorious conditions required by heaven as an offering of indemnity representing your entire clan, such as the Kim clan or the Park clan. He may also call a family and command them to step forward as an offering of indemnity representing the entire family of 30 million people before heaven. Furthermore, He may command a certain tribe to become an offering of indemnity to pave the way for this nation, this country, and this world to survive.  
He may instruct a certain nation to take on the mission and responsibility of indemnity to restore heaven and earth and step forward as an offering. If at that time such a command is given to our Korean people, we must be able to say that the entire nation will go forth as commanded. Without going through this process from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and country, we cannot unfold the path of restoration history to a global victory. This is a fact we know all too well.  
Today, most people living on earth desire glory without effort and hope for the results of victory without exertion. However, even if they achieve results of victory and obtain glory in the human world, it may be recognized in the human realm, but heaven and earth cannot acknowledge it. Why? Because indemnity conditions remain. This is because there is an official program by which God governs according to the principles of indemnity and restoration.  
When we consider this from a principled standpoint, among the churches facing the end times, which denomination is going through the process of becoming a global offering on behalf of the nation? If the Unification Church has emerged to fulfill such a mission, our Unification Church’s connection is linked to heaven and earth beyond representing the Korean people. We must clearly understand that such a connection exists.  
From this standpoint, after swearing before heaven and allowing Satan to enter, when we offer the offerings that God desires, if even Satan can acknowledge them, then we can say that we have become a substance that meets the conditions required by God. Only such a being can make Satan submit. When this happens, you will develop from the individual to the family, then to the nation, and finally to the world.  
The reason for being struck until the limit is reached  
When we look at history from this perspective, God labored for 2,000 years after the fall of Adam to establish Abraham, and after Abraham, through Isaac, Jacob established the name Israel on earth, thereby finally establishing a victorious nation. The victory at that time was both the victory of Jacob’s generation and the foundation for familial victory. It means that victory was achieved in the world of Satan.  
To achieve victory, what must be done? One must enter the world of Satan and be struck. Jacob being deceived ten times in the household of Laban, which represented the world of Satan, is equivalent to being struck ten times. However, Jacob patiently waited until he could stand before heaven’s will. Noah did the same. Grandfather Noah also endured for 120 years and was faithful before God. After 120 years, God informed Noah that He would judge the world and commanded him to build the ark on the top of Mount Ararat. Why did God give such a command? This command, when viewed from a common sense perspective, is not normal. One should build a boat by the riverside or at the beach, so why was he commanded to build it on a mountain? This was a strategy to position Noah in a place where the entire populace of that time could oppose him. Among the people of that time, there was no one who did not judge Noah with words. One must stand in such a position. Grandfather Noah was ridiculed and scorned by men and women of all ages for 120 years as he built the ark, and they kicked him and did all sorts of things to him. This was to position him in a place where Satan could symbolically and literally do whatever he wanted.  
Those whom God loves and establishes must be struck first in the world of Satan. If one is struck first in the world of Satan, then one can strike the world of Satan. Judgment is done this way. After allowing the beloved sons and daughters of God to be struck first, then Satan is struck. This was true for Noah, and Jacob, who established the foundation of victory known as Israel, also reclaimed what was his after being deceived in Laban’s house. Moses was the same, and so was Jesus.  
When Jesus came to this earth, he came as the Messiah, but to truly be the Messiah, he must be able to judge the world. If he cannot carry out the act of judgment, he cannot become the Messiah. Why? Because this earth is under Satan’s dominion, and without judgment, he cannot be recognized as the King of Kings in this world. Therefore, if he came to the earth as the Messiah, he must judge the world.  
So how must one judge? One must receive the attacks of Satan. Jesus, despite being pursued and chased, being the leader of the nation, should have been pursued along with the nation. If that had been the case, he would not have died. However, because only Jesus was pursued, he ended up dying. Jesus should have stood in a position of being pursued before the world of Satan, but because he could not stand in that position, the history of Israel was cut off. That is why Christians who believe in Jesus must become a group that is pursued in the historical course. They must be pursued until the end when Jesus returns to this earth. They must face the consequences of having driven Jesus out with the authority of the second Israel. They must be struck personally, familially, tribally, nationally, and globally. Right now, we are in a process of facing the world.  
Because this is the path of indemnity and restoration, heaven restores as much as one is struck. Heaven can strike as much as Satan strikes.  
In the late 20th century, the Unification Church emerged, proclaiming a new ideology. If this gathering and this group have come forth to carry out the historical path of restoration for heaven and have come bearing the mission of a new era according to heaven’s strategy, then they must first be struck. They must be overwhelmed. They must endure all persecutions and sufferings of the world. Beyond the nationalistic ideologies and traditional national standards, now is a global era, so they must be overwhelmed by global ideologies and standards. They must be struck until the limit is reached.  
That is why today, the lives of the Unification Church and its members are re-enacting a historical tragedy that will leave a mark for eternity. This must unfold personally, familially, tribally, nationally, and globally. After that, heaven will cause us to be overwhelmed based on national standards before the world stage. Only when we establish ourselves there can we finally surpass the standards of global judgment. This is the history of restoration.  
The final war, the final loyal soldiers  
Now is the time to move beyond the personal era and towards the family, tribe, nation, and country. They say so, right? You may not know, but this time corresponds to the time when the Israelite nation welcomed Jesus. Looking at the situation in Korea, it fits perfectly. So what will happen to this nation that persecutes heaven and drives out God’s beloved sons and daughters? Ultimately, they will find themselves in the same position. Those who drive out the people of heaven may initially appear bold and confident, believing they can do as they please, but in the end, they will find themselves in a more miserable position than the people of heaven. 22) The Historical Path of Golgotha 
<Summary of the Words> Because the human ancestors fell, there remains sorrow in this universe regarding the past and present, and God has endured infinite hardships to resolve this sorrow throughout history. 
The life of an individual is infinitely precious. The value of this life is only revealed through the process of living a heavenly life. In our daily lives, we can either manifest the true value of ourselves or allow the opposite to happen. 
You must achieve true and valuable victorious values in your daily life. The value of goodness that appears here must be possessed by you.
The conditions of sorrow and death will pass by you when the time comes. Just as the sorrow of Adam and Eve remains the sorrow of the whole, your joy, mistakes, or sadness also become part of the whole. It is difficult to recover from a day's mistakes in a year. Even if we perform a good deed for a day, true satisfaction does not come from that alone. True satisfaction comes when the standard is established that can transcend from the individual to the family, society, nation, world, and even to the universe. We must understand that God is urging this through our hearts.

August 18, 1964 (Tuesday), at the summit of Bukak Mountain, Seoul.
* This message has been summarized from the 12th issue of <Gyeonggi Frontline>, with the title added by the editor.

God did not come to Noah and Abraham to resolve the sorrow of the whole, but to alleviate personal sorrow. Therefore, when they sought the path of personal sacrifice and stood at the place of sacrifice, only then did God also call that individual and labor together until the work of sacrifice was completed. The mistakes of Noah's family did not stop at one person's fault, and Abraham's mistakes also did not remain as personal errors. These mistakes and wrongs piled up and overlapped, leading Jesus to walk the path of suffering as the substantial offering. The cross of Jesus further intensified God's sorrow. The path of restoration becomes increasingly difficult as time passes. For this reason, God ultimately could not help but offer His only begotten Son. Although God did not show sorrow before those who killed His only begotten Son, His heart was endlessly sad.

The 30 million people of Korea standing on the path of restoration must walk a miserable path, just as Moses drove the Israelite nation out before the forces of Satan, represented by Pharaoh. It is the members of the Unification Church who must fulfill the mission of the priesthood in such a position. The path you are walking is the historical Golgotha of world history. Have you ever thought about what would have happened if Jesus' disciple had been a woman instead of a man? Before a perfect woman can appear, a perfect man must manifest. Only when Jesus appears as a perfect man and Satan can no longer present conditions for accusation does a perfect woman come to be. Thus, the Lord of the Second Advent seeks to establish humanity as brides, having completed the ideal of creation, allowing them to shed the conditions for Satan's accusations and appear victorious.

As the world today divides into two, Korea is also divided in this way. God has discerned through the history of repetition centered around the numbers three and four. Just as Cain and Abel were divided, our church may also divide. If our group were to split into two, where would you belong? You must prepare your own self. The time must come to establish the principles of heaven's providence. The Bible says not to swear, but we must live a life of swearing.

The future judgment will take place through the three processes of the Word, heart, and character. Have you ever shed tears to the point of your skin being worn out for heaven? The center for fulfilling the Word, establishing heart, and completing character is the Teacher, and the center of the Teacher is God. 

When a great historical event occurs, a great movement takes place. If you follow the setting sun, you cannot catch up. Therefore, you must go in reverse. Look a little longer! An even greater battlefield will unfold. However, we must go toward the world stage seeking God in a fully united form. 

If your mistakes are passed down to your descendants, it becomes more difficult to restore. You are in a time when you can achieve perfection, so if you do well, you can achieve it; however, if you stumble, your descendants will have to go through the path of rebirth, growth, and completion again, making it even more difficult. 

Have you ever experienced the love that God had for Adam and Eve? You are in a blessed position due to the benefits of the times. Adam and Eve did not have the Day of All Things, the Day of Children, or the Day of Parents, but you have all of these, so you are in a blessed position. Even if you do not receive the same love from God as Adam and Eve, being on the path of restoration is a blessing. 

This is the time when you are transformed from being adopted in the Lord's name into true children, crossing over the summit of Golgotha. Jesus resurrected after three days and ascended to heaven, but we must restore the number four on earth. Only then will God be pleased. The roots must not appear outwardly. 

You must evangelize at least three people a day. If you cannot do that, you should pray for at least three hours. When the environment suppresses you, you should pray to conquer that environment. Only then can you save the nation. 

Only truth can bring back truth.
<Summary of the Message> The Bible says not to worry about what to eat, what to drink, or what to wear, but to seek only the kingdom. God has been working to establish that kingdom by placing humans in it. 

Originally, Adam was an individual representing the whole. Because that Adam was lost, God lost the whole. Therefore, God has been working to find the whole by establishing one Adam. God is seeking those who wish to live in the homeland that the human heart desires. 

Such people had to go through a process of trials. Noah faced great trials, but he overcame that environment with a single-mindedness toward God. If Noah had worried about what to eat, what to wear, or what to drink, he would not have been able to fulfill what God commanded. Without worrying about such things, Noah managed to persevere for 120 years. 

In Abraham's family, both husband and wife believed in God, and the wife, Sarah, absolutely obeyed her husband; thus, even in difficult trials, their hearts did not change, allowing them to become the ancestors of faith. 

Jacob also endured trials for 21 years, and Moses led the nation through trials. Jesus also had to overcome global trials along with the Israelite nation. 

However, Israel, which had to gather the entire world of Christianity to establish one nation, dreamed only of the nation that Israel desired and fell. 

At that time, Christian believers hoped for heaven, but there were no people who wanted to become heavenly citizens. In other words, while there were those who wished to enter heaven, there were none who were willing to take responsibility for establishing and maintaining heaven. 

We, who are in the position of the Third Israel, must seek that kingdom before anything else. A tribe without a homeland cannot exist. If Jesus had established Israel and entered Rome, he would not have died. 

God wishes to settle the fallen culture and history of the past, and all Christian believers have the mission to do so. If they cannot fulfill that mission, then it falls to us, the members of the Unification Church, to accomplish it. 

From this perspective, we should not live today as we did yesterday, nor should we live tomorrow as we do today. The greater the mission given to us, the more trials and struggles increase proportionately. We cannot rely solely on content; we must have results. 

In this end-time era, when we ask if there is anyone who can represent the world, we must be able to say, "Here I am." We need people who can represent the world more than ten million others. What remains for such a person? It is loyalty. Only loyalty. 

A prisoner suffers to atone for his own sins, but we suffer to atone for the sins of the nation.
