To become a victor of the four-year course, one must win with heart, win with character, win with truth, and win with action. 
When you do not practice the teacher's commands, the teacher who spoke the words must take responsibility and cannot avoid indemnity. The one who humbly accepted this course was Jesus. That was what made Jesus the Lord. 
The teacher humbly accepted the advice of a child and even asked the spiritualists how God sees him. It is more important to be a companion of heart who would not change even if given heaven and earth than to be a capable and skilled leader. 
Once that time has passed, regretting it will be too late. Anyone can live just as they please. However, the question is how much value one lives with. Whether one lives with personal value, national value, or heavenly value determines that value. 
Abel must set Cain before God to receive blessings. And Cain must receive Abel's blessings. Are there three Cains centered around the earth? Are there three Cains centered around oneself? If Cain says he is tired, it is because he does not know, so he must be informed. The path of restoration is not one that is walked alone but together. 
From now on, there is no need to recover the weary. In the past, faith was about following Abel, but now it must be about serving him. 
If one cannot directly evangelize, even a Cain who has faith through me must be raised. 
Can someone who is worse than Cain become Abel? 
Abel must give to Cain. What will he give? 
Now is the time to put sincerity into prayer again. During this revival period, you must be resolute. When you pray, you must be able to enter a realm where you lose your consciousness. When touching the world of heart, it cannot be done without tears. 
One must be a person who has established a heavenly life to enter the actual heaven. That heaven is only realized when a Cain-like family connects with Abel-like true children and true families. 
You must have a place to lie down, a place to stand, and a place to work in heaven to establish a connection with heaven. 
Will you lose your mission because the issues of eating and dressing are difficult, and sell the blessings given by God for money? Is that your intention? God's blessings cannot be exchanged for anything, even if He gives heaven and earth. 
From now on, having completed various rituals at the headquarters, if you work only with a heart-centered standard, you will achieve results. Do not criticize the work the teacher is doing. Can you know what will happen in several years or decades? Do you know how much effort has been put into sorting out the complex spiritual environment to achieve what we have today? 
If it is work centered on God, the teacher has accepted whatever anyone does. The teacher has now fulfilled his responsibility. Where will I remain now? That place is a place of heart. 
Time flows, and the teacher's sorrow is that he could not leave all the feelings he held in this world. How much will this world, which has not been able to shed tears with the teacher over the historical sorrow, regret? 
This mountain and river know all the teacher's hardships. Therefore, if the teacher cannot see the day of joy, this mountain and river cannot rejoice either. Having blessed all the famous scenic spots, now even the mountains and trees there must have no grievances. 
When looking at six thousand years of history, one's life is like a dot. In this moment, think about what you must do. 
In teaching any work, it must be taught with heart. 
Is there anyone you can love as much as your own body? You must have people, regions, and churches that you love. If the family members do not fulfill the teacher's standards, the teacher must bear that burden alone. 
Let us become necessary people. 
<Summary of the Message> Above all, God needed humans the most. This is because happiness and glory can only be enjoyed through humans. God first needs individuals, but furthermore, He needs families, lineages, nations, and even heaven and earth. 
God has endured and carried out His providence through all kinds of difficulties and pains. Among the things needed, the most necessary is that I must find myself. I must endure all difficulties to become the existence that heaven hopes for, even if it takes one year or two years to globalize myself. 
What does the ideology of the Unification Church require? First, it requires the sons and daughters of God. Second, it requires the families, lineages, nations, worlds, and heaven and earth established by the sons and daughters of God. 
To receive blessings as an individual, one must ensure that their family lives well. The earth must be able to face me, and I must also become a necessary person for that earth. 
I must also be a being that can say, "I need God." While success is good, it must be a success for the nation and the world. 
During this six-month evangelism period, the district leader of Chungbuk must hold revival meetings as much as the teacher needs, and all members of the district must resonate with this. 
On October 1, 1964, at noon, at the Cheongju Church. 
* This message was given during the dedication ceremony of the Chungbuk district headquarters church and has been compiled from what was published in "Seonghwa," Issue 40 (October 1, 1964). The title was added by the editor. 
Heavenly Warriors
We Unification Church members say we are family, right? What does the term "family" mean? If we break it down, it means "mouths that eat together." So, a family is brothers and sisters who eat together, a family that shares meals. Everyone is a mother and father, and siblings. 
Reflections from Daegu
So, from the perspective of the Unification Church teacher, where is the eternal paradise where our family can live? How does it feel to live there? Does Korea feel like an eternal paradise? Even if it is not Korea, there must be a place somewhere that is an eternal paradise. Everyone, wouldn't it be nice if such an eternal paradise exists? "Yes." But what if it doesn't exist? "We must create it." Create it? Who will create it? "We will." Is everyone confident? "Yes." It will not be created just by suffering without purpose. 
So how will we create it? 
"Oh, beautiful mountains and seas!" That sounds good. The mountains and rivers of Korea are beautiful. Even looking around the world, there are few countries that receive as many benefits from nature as Korea does. Everywhere is picturesque. Beautiful mountains and seas! My beloved hometown! Do you all have a beloved hometown? "Yes." Really? When flies are buzzing and there are bad smells, what happens? Young ladies will all run away. But has that hometown become dear to you? Farmers must become attached to their land. 
As the teacher travels around, when he arrives in Daegu, the impression is very different. The feeling of going to Jeolla Province and Gyeongsang Province is very different. But among Gyeongsang Province, Daegu leaves the deepest impression. In terms of cities in Gyeongsang Province, where does Daegu rank? Second, right? But in the teacher's mind, it feels like the first city. It is because he loves it. Daegu is a place that cannot be forgotten in the teacher's mind. Whenever he thinks of Daegu, he remembers the time over ten years ago when he prayed, resolved, and vowed with a great heart. He thinks of the time when he said, "Whenever we talk about Daegu, let’s fight magnificently and fulfill God's moment." It is a place that he cannot forget. Do you all like it? "Yes." 
So, the Unification Church members living here must also experience hardships. If you are a Unification Church believer who claims to establish the way of loyalty in front of the will, representing Daegu and even Gyeongsangbuk-do, you must all go out. What activities will you engage in? I want to try something like judo, throwing people around. Why? Because to bring Daegu into our will, we must be able to freely control all of Daegu. 
Can this be done alone? No. So, our young men,
I am trying to mobilize young ladies to demonstrate my skills. I intend to give commands. To do this, I need courage proportional to the resentment that this teacher felt in the past. What is needed are men and women who have the ability to resolve the teacher's past grievances.

As I came to Daegu today, I thought about what I should say. Should I say something good, or something bitter? It seemed that I had to say something bitter. However, how can I do that? I dislike bad words. I must suppress my feelings of disappointment and speak good words for you. How pitiful is that? At times like this, I can feel that God must have had such feelings.

Parents are the same, right? Even when their children do wrong, they cannot vent their anger because they love them and have grown attached to them, so they speak good words. You can feel this too.

Today, I thought about cursing in one word. Everyone, would you like to hear a curse? Will you listen? You in Daegu must always be aware of such things. Last time, we held revival meetings in the first, second, and third phases, right? We will do it again. And now, although the Gyeongbuk district headquarters is the most shabby, I will build a larger Unification Church here in Daegu than any other church. People of Gyeongbuk, isn't that glorious? "Yes."

People from Daegu are spineless. They are soft. But don’t take it the wrong way, people from Daegu. People without bones are like the people from Daegu, right? People from Gyeongbuk are like those without husbands.

As I came straight from Chungbuk through Gyeongnam to Daegu, I felt bad from the alleys. But I endured it. So, I cannot walk freely in Daegu. You probably feel the same way. When you sit, you must sit quietly. Why? Because if a big person sits down, there will be no room left.

People are needed
Everyone, among our church districts, the Daegu district headquarters is the most shabby. So what about the people who come into this shabby headquarters? Are they shabby? Are they pitiful? You cannot say that. If you say it’s pitiful, you will hear something, so you have no choice but to remain silent. In the future, the Gyeongbuk district, that is, Daegu Church, will be the largest. Do you think this way? Do you have such thoughts? No? You should respond. Even if you don’t, when the teacher asks, you should know how to answer "Yes." How about it? Will you do that? Will you not? "We will." When? When will you do it? Are you just thinking about it in your heart? That won’t do. You must do it in reality.

When you go to our headquarters church, it is magnificent, right? Those who have been to the headquarters church know. The headquarters church is magnificent, right? The teacher lives in such a magnificent house. When I go to Seoul, there are many tiny houses nearby. I want to throw a few thousand billion won to build all the houses at once. When I have money, I want to close my eyes and do that first. Right now, I cannot see it at all with my eyes open.

I do not want such a big house. That’s enough. What I want now is people, not houses. I need people who can fight evil for the sake of good, people who can sacrifice their lives for their purpose. This Gyeongbuk district headquarters may be shabby, but what about the people of Gyeongsangbuk-do? What do people from Seoul say about the people of Gyeongsangbuk-do? They call them barley idiots.

If you look closely, the people from Gyeongsang-do who are in politics fight at the doorstep. After a big fight, they should unite at the door, but they scatter instead. Is that so or not? But the people from Jeolla-do do the opposite; they negotiate at the door and then fight after entering. That is the characteristic of the people from Jeolla-do compared to the people from Gyeongsang-do.

At times in the restoration process, the temperament of the people from Gyeongsang-do is needed. However, today, when fighting against the great powers, we must establish a strategic plan and take a full offensive, so we must unite. People must unite. But what need is there for a house? No matter how good a king of a country is at fighting, can he win against many enemies? Therefore, we need people. To save the country, we need people, not houses. We need people.

Currently, they say Korea is going downhill, but it is not because there are no good houses in Korea. It is because there are no people. It is not because there are no scholars or doctors that Korea has become like this. There are people, but the problem is that they cannot unite. The older gentlemen hold their beards and say, "Oh! What do you know? You must listen to us. What should we do for our elders!" And the young people complain that there is a generation gap with their grandparents. They cannot become one. That cannot happen. We must set one goal and have hope for it, and while developing one movement, we must destroy everything that does not align with that goal. We must become people who can do this. Do you understand?

So, dear members of Gyeongsangbuk-do, there is no need to boast about having a big house, and there is no need to worry about having a small house. As I mentioned earlier, the headquarters church is big, right? But what the teacher wants is not a house. More than a house, I desire people, and I hope to dress people rather than decorate the house. When dressing, it should be the inside rather than the outside. Then, no one can take my inside away. Not even God can take it away. You must become a person who can say that.

No matter how great a person in the world is, you must become a person who cannot have their inside taken away. Once you decide in your heart or make a vow and lock your heart, you must become a person whom no one can open, a person who can open only themselves, and a person who can unite for one purpose. This is the kind of person we need.

As I came to Daegu and looked around, I feel very good when I see young people more than many others. Do you remember when the teacher said that the first generation has passed and the second generation has come? I don’t know if the pastors or elders from established churches have come, but they may oppose the Unification Church until their foreheads are bald and their hair falls out, until they turn gray. However, their sons and daughters will come into the hands of Teacher Moon. This is the firm belief that the Unification Church holds.

Even if the first generation falls in the wilderness and becomes food for eagles, I will be needed for the second generation. The established church pastors or elders who oppose this may feel disappointed, but I think this way. If you have the confidence to oppose my thoughts, come out. Let’s see who wins. This is what I believe, and even God cannot take it away. No matter who opposes or mobilizes the power of the country to oppose, it cannot be helped. Let’s see if it works or not.

That is why the Unification Church is the church of the second generation. It must be unshakeable wherever it goes. Even if it is kicked hard, it should only roll without changing. Even if it rolls, it should not scatter but should roll together, growing bigger. I like such people. A ball that rolls when kicked is good.

Sometimes, the teacher may kick the young men and women of the Unification Church. I will kick the young ones once in a while.

Resilient and proactive people
Then it will hit a rock. A truly solid person will hit a big rock and bleed, but they will not break; instead, they will bury the rock pieces and fall. Do you understand what I mean? Now that I have come to Gyeongbuk, I hope to kick you all to where the rocks are. How about it? If I kick with my foot, will your head break and your body break, and will you just fall straight down? You must remain unshaken. We must create such warriors.

What is the ideology of our Unification Church? It is unification, right? To achieve unification, we need strength. We need capability. If we have beauty like the creation and shine brightly, there will be no one who does not need us. We must shine. We must shine strongly. It is not enough to be strong alone. We must be resilient. Such individuals are needed, and at the same time, such groups are needed.

We need people who can run freely even when woven this way and that. They should not be so stiff that they break when hit. They must be flexible enough to stand up no matter how they are woven.

Then what will we do? Sometimes, I take young men and women to the sea. There are many fish in the sea. There are fish that fly and fish that float. We must catch those fish, but how will we catch them? Will we catch them by fishing every day, or will we throw a net the size of a palm? In places like Alaska in the U.S. or Japan, or in the Pacific Ocean, when we throw a net to catch all the fish there, I sometimes think I would like to be the one handling the line.

Otherwise, I would like to drop an atomic bomb in the Pacific Ocean to make all the fish float and cause a fish disaster. There must be various methods. How to catch them depends on how we think.

Our Unification Church is the same. We want to shake the world centered around our nation. We want to shake the world centered around the three thousand ri peninsula. In the Far East, Korea is a very poor country. Although it has three thousand ri of territory, a white-clad nation, and beautiful mountains, it is a pitiful country. However, although it grew up pitifully, the Unification Church has set out to create a shining content that is not pitiful. Isn’t that right?

What will happen if the white-clad nation collides with the world? A year ago, our nation would have been shattered. But now it is different. With 120 countries opposing the Unification Church, what kind of group will remain in the end when colliding with so many countries? It will be the group of the Unification Church. The group of the Unification Church will remain until the end. How about it? Isn’t it embarrassing? Isn’t it embarrassing that a small group of the Unification Church remains after confronting so many countries? Why aren’t you answering? Have you resolved to keep your mouth shut when the teacher asks from now on?

The Unification Church is a church of resilient and proactive people. Even if we have no money, when we say let’s do something, we do it all. When we say let’s make money, we make it fiercely. However, saving the country does not depend on money. We need people. We need very fierce people. We need people who have the conviction to discern and judge, regardless of whether democracy, communism, or any other ideology sweeps in. Of course, I feel sorry for the older people, but we do not need grandfathers and grandmothers with gray hair. Please do not feel disappointed, older folks. I am also getting older. We need young people, young men and women overflowing with passion and spirit. If we unite around such young people, we can dominate the world.

Are the people of Gyeongsangbuk-do willing to join such a cause? Raise your hands if you are willing. Oh! Put them down.

We are the warriors of heaven
Then let’s sing the fourth verse of the song "Warriors of Heaven." (Singing) Where are we advancing to? What kind of world? The world of our homeland. Where is that world? It is the brilliant culture that rises in the East. Is your current position brilliant? What is the whole world? It refers not only to Korea but to the entire world.

Anyone with the name of a person can enter. Regardless of the past, present, or future, anyone who is a person belongs to the whole world. What is all humanity? Brothers? If they are brothers, that would be a big deal. When asked how many brothers someone has, they say many. They worry because they have many younger siblings who keep taking from them. They say they have to send them off to get married and prepare a household, and they are at their wits' end. What if all humanity becomes brothers? What will happen? If all humanity truly becomes brothers, what will happen? Will such a person need brothers? Have you thought about this?

Everyone! Do you need such brothers? Do you really need them? How much? As much as the whole world? Yes, we need them. Absolutely. How much do we need them? We need them enough to sacrifice our lives. Why? Because without those people, those brothers, we cannot form a great lineage of good. A lineage of good cannot be formed with just one person. It cannot be formed with just one nation. People of all colors, regardless of being white, black, or yellow, must all become brothers. Everyone must mix and become brothers.

Then what is a brother? Is it enough to look similar to be brothers? Is it enough to eat together to be brothers? Is it enough to wear the same clothes like twins to be brothers? No. They must share the same bloodline to be brothers. Next, they must have the same parents. Of course, there must be parents for a bloodline to exist. What is the most essential requirement to become brothers? It is having the same parents. They must have the same parents to be brothers. There are half-brothers, right? And there are sworn brothers too? But what kind of brothers must they be? They must be full-blooded brothers. How about it? Are you confident you can become full-blooded brothers? That is the problem.

What is the center of the ideal world we desire, the new world that will be realized in the future, and the new cultural world that will shine brilliantly across the globe? It is the True Parents, the True Parents of humanity. That is why the good parents we desire must be honored forever. There is a wide range of honoring. Therefore, we must honor them from a holistic perspective. And thus, we sing, "Surely, we will achieve, one world."

We humans were originally born as the protagonists of one world, whether as sons or daughters of one family, to govern the world freely and live ruling over the universe. However, due to the fall, we could not do so. Therefore, we are trying to restore that world.

Surely, we will achieve  
What kind of world? A world of two? No, it is "Surely, we will achieve, one world."  
Then what kind of world is one world? It is a unified world. Until now, when looking at the Unification Church, day and night, Teacher Moon has been struggling alone in Korea, and people thought he was not a person, but if they thought so, they were mistaken. I have this thought about the pastors of established churches. Just wait and see. Stagnant water eventually becomes foul. The trends of the times will reveal our words. No matter how much effort and loyalty have been put into raising people throughout history, they will return overnight. I have come out with confidence.

Let’s wait and see. The faith perspectives claimed by established churches, both old and new, and the faith perspectives claimed by scholars and doctors, as well as the faith perspectives claimed by various churches, will eventually collide with and be absorbed by our ideology of unification and the faith perspective of our Unification Church. You will see.

Have you ever flown a kite? When you fly a kite, if you coat the string with powdered glass, it flies pleasantly in the wind. But if a shabby kite flies next to it, it will be cut off without a doubt. That is how it should be. Let’s see which side’s line will break when we collide with the anchor line of heaven connected to our Unification group and the anchor line of established churches. The line of good based on justice will win.
So what kind of world is a unified world? It is a unified world, indeed. In that unified world, God also likes to be present within it. Therefore, even if we ask Him to come out a bit, He remains still. There is a reason for that. The Lord, who comes as the true parents of humanity and brings the ideal of the Second Advent, also earnestly wishes to come out. However, it is clear that He will not come out.

Truly, it will be realized, a unified world. This is the strange aspect of our Unification Church. Those who have tasted the essence of the Unification Church do not wish to leave from the day they step in. Just like a bee that knows the taste of honey. They bury their heads in it and keep buzzing around. Once a bee has tasted honey, it will try to pull its stinger out with a pair of tweezers. Then its body will fall off. Yet, it still does not leave. The teacher knows this well from observing bees. Our Unification Church members must be like that. Once they have tasted it, no one can call them to come back. They come on their own. I came to Daegu today, but did anyone call me to come? I am saying not to go just because someone calls you. You should go with a clear purpose based on your own judgment. Once you have tasted it, there is no need for anyone to say come or go. Even if they say do not come, you will come. Therefore, I am thinking of trying to persecute them so that they cannot enter our church. "Do you want to attend the Unification Church?" 

Thus, we must create a world where ideological brothers, centered on heaven, love one another. The people of the world, the brothers of the world, are fallen brothers. They are brothers who have received the lineage of Satan and have sullied their bloodline. However, when the group of true brothers centered on the true connection of heaven collides with the group of the world, which side must be cut off? Sorry, but the connection with the brothers of the world, that is, the brothers who are your blood relatives, must be severed. There must be something stronger than worldly connections to actively operate this world. Do you think unification can happen without such an active force? It cannot.

Are the people gathered here fully equipped with such strength? They are gathered here to equip themselves.

Truly, it will be realized, a unified world. Who said this? Truly, it will be realized, a unified world! Is this something that others do? We must achieve it. Through our bodies and our minds, truly, it will be realized, a unified world. This is how it should be.

With that, such groups must become brothers, and we must be proud, warriors of unification. What is there to be proud of? The hopeful work that no one in the world has accomplished, the work that no one has handled throughout the history of mankind, which can resolve the grievances of all people and the grievances of the entire universe, and can become the cornerstone for fulfilling wishes—how joyful is that? Therefore, we are proud, warriors of unification. A warrior refers to a person equipped with the spirit, courage, and trained equipment to defeat countless enemies. We are proud, warriors of unification. We are the warriors of unification, vigorously advancing toward the unified world. Now, let those who want to advance raise their hands. Alright, that’s enough. Let’s sing once more. Heavenly Warriors, start! (Singing)

What was the title of the song we just sang? "Heavenly Warriors." Did we not say we must become heavenly warriors? To become heavenly warriors, first, we must understand God's heart. To be a loyal subject of the nation, one must understand the heart of the king, and to be a filial child before parents, one must understand the heart of the father and mother. Similarly, to be a heavenly warrior, one must understand God's heart. We must understand God's heart before creation, God's heart at the time of creation, and also the sorrowful heart of God when humanity fell after creation, and the heart of restoration that weaves through the history of restoration while holding that sorrowful heart. Additionally, we must understand the heart that hopes for the world after restoration.

Today, people who believe in Jesus say they will go to heaven, but how wonderful it would be if that were the case? They say that if you believe, you will be saved, but what is the content of that belief? Is it just believing? Will you believe while abandoning your nation and the world? What is the limit of faith? Is it just a vague belief that you will be saved if you believe? Is reciting prayers also a form of belief? When asked about the limits of faith, they cannot answer and just groan.

Believing is not such an easy thing. To believe, to what extent must one believe? One must believe all the way to the back alleys of God's heart, to the very edge of God's wishes. Faith is not just a game done out of necessity. How pitiful is it? Have you ever seen a father saying to his children, "I am your father, so believe me"? Would a delinquent believe if I said, "I am truly your father, so believe me"? How pitiful is God? He tells His children to believe in Him, to believe in Him, and how pitiful is that?

Heaven is a world of heart.

So how should we believe in God? What are God's circumstances when dealing with individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world? What is God's heart when fighting against Satan, and what are God's wishes? We must know and believe these things. But until now, who has known this?

They say they will go to heaven by believing in Jesus? If that were the case, why not go to the heavenly throne and command? It does not work that way. When I went to the spirit world, it was not like that. I tried to meet the Korean pastors who were said to have believed well on earth, but I could not find them anywhere. Upon inquiry, I found they were far away. If you want to go to heaven, you should go. Those of you who have joined the Unification Church should not try to follow the path that mainstream Christians believe leads to heaven. Heaven is not a place you can simply go to. Even searching thoroughly in the spirit world, it is not like that.

We must understand God's heart from the time of creation. What must God's heart have been like when He created everything from a single blade of grass? How joyful must He have been to see each created being blossom with the devotion He put into creating them? We must understand that heart, the heart of God at the time of creation. Look for this content in theological books. Is there anything like this? Even if you look at all the theological books in the world, you will not find it. So how can we understand what God's heart was like at the time of creation?

Jesus declared on this earth, "I have come to cast fire upon the earth, and if it is already kindled, what do I wish?" (Luke 12:49). He also said, "I have a baptism to undergo, and how distressed I am until it is accomplished." Why was He distressed? Because the Jewish people were wrong, and it was necessary to correct that or completely eradicate it. That is why He is still facing various humiliations today. Thus, we must establish patience.

Since the time of the Liberal Party until now, how much effort has been made to eliminate the Unification Church through three administrations? However, the Unification Church is not so easily dealt with. The teacher speaking here is someone who cannot be overcome even by 3 billion people. No matter what anyone says, they cannot make me submit. No matter how logical the theories presented are, I have no ideology that I can concede to. I cannot answer the questions I pose. However, I am confident in answering their questions. I live with this kind of confidence. Such confidence is necessary on the path of faith. The heart of God that our Unification Church speaks of is long, great, and deep. We must understand God's heart before creation, God's heart at the time of creation, and God's heart when Adam and Eve fell after creation. We must understand how much of a nail Adam and Eve drove into God's heart when they fell. We must also understand how much God has grieved after the fall. Additionally, we must understand how much sorrowful heart God has while walking the path of restoration, pushing His sons and daughters into the depths of tragic death and urging them to endure. We must understand how sorrowful God's heart must have been. Thus, through the final central being, we must resolve this sinful world and release God's heart of sorrow.

Look at the Bible all day long. Is there such content? Is there God's heart? That is why we are told to pray in the end times. We are told to anoint ourselves and enter into a secret place to pray.

The heart that our Unification Church speaks of is the heart of hope that all humanity desires, the heart that must connect all people, and the heart that God has been seeking until now. In that realm, it can encompass all of heaven and earth and can embrace the entirety. Therefore, to become a heavenly warrior, first, we must go through this heart. Then, the person becomes an issue.

However, Adam and Eve, due to their fall, became unaware of God's heart. If Adam and Eve had grown and perfected their character and had drawn closer to God, if they had entered into a mature stage as perfected beings, God would have blessed them and bestowed His heart upon them. Thus, He intended to create a heavenly couple who could connect with God's love and heart to establish a lineage-based family.

Originally, Adam and Eve were to inherit such an immense heart of God and become the true ancestors of humanity on the foundation of heart. Thus, their descendants were to be able to dominate this world. However, humanity lost that foundation of heart, which is called the fall. Consequently, people became unable to receive God's heart. They lost God's heart, lost the character that could resemble God's heart, and lost the purpose of the Word that should be established on character.

The three criteria for judgment.

That is why, in the end times, judgment will be based on heart, character, and the Word. It will not be judged by how well one believed. God has a central heart. There is a single central heart that God must establish, centered on heaven and earth. And there is a central character that can become one with this heart of God. Furthermore, there is a central Word that can speak on behalf of God, which can become one with this character and heart. These are the three criteria for judgment.

Among these, the judgment of the Word occurs first. In the fallen world of humanity, the judgment of the Word occurs first. What does the fallen world seek today? It seeks the world of truth. What does the history that develops alongside culture seek? It seeks an ideology that can lead to a cultural world. Until now, the trends of the world have emerged through ideologies and doctrines, but they are floundering in a dead end without establishing a standard of the Word that can unify all people and bring harmony. This is the current reality.

When You ask who will love this land of Korea and all of humanity in this world, we have long since resolved in our hearts that we must be the first to respond. We earnestly hope and desire that all our commitments will remain unwavering and steadfast.  
Now, the final times are rapidly changing. We know that we have gathered here through a historical connection. Therefore, today we must overcome, and tomorrow we must pioneer; let us become heavenly warriors who can pledge today’s victory and tomorrow’s pioneering. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
O my Father, who has protected this body even in tribulation! I know for certain that You command me to go even when I am in despair and You give me orders to move forward. I have already followed Your commands and have endured harsh environments, but Your will is mysterious, and Your providence is truly wondrous.  
O Father! When difficulties arise, I have come to know that behind them, You always bring gifts. I have learned that You love those who endure persecution and bless those who overcome, so I ask You to remember the sincerity of today’s family, who look to You with all their hearts, and do not forsake them. I earnestly hope and desire this. May the paths of those who weep bring forth flowers in the garden of Your heart, and may they be made to become shields of victory on the path of the cross that You have left behind.  
This period is one we have sworn before You, and now the workers of unification are spread throughout, fulfilling Your words and the history of Your new life. O Father! Please shine a new, brilliant light upon this nation. We must become the fuse that ignites the fire for countless young men and women who are captured by the powers of darkness, so please guide us with Your almighty power during this opportunity. I earnestly hope and desire this.  
Now we stand on the path of return that we must take; whether we die or live, we must go. May You be with us, Father, so that even if we fall, we can testify to You and receive testimony from You, and may we become Your sons and daughters. O Father! I earnestly hope and desire this.  
Father, bless the Gyeongbuk region, and especially grant great grace to the city of Daegu. May all matters that come and go not be for my sake. May all things be for You, and for the purpose of establishing loyalty before You, and for Your will, so I earnestly hope and desire that You will gather them. Please allow nothing to be for the sake of humanity, and since we have begun with You, may we bear fruit as Yours. I also earnestly hope and desire that we may become heavenly warriors who prepare a foundation of victory that countless saints in the spirit world can rejoice in.  
We thank You for granting us this time today. While we thank You for what we have encountered during this period, we also thank You for allowing us to become one before You. Moreover, we, who must be grateful for both life and death centered on Your will, are already those who have resolved to risk our lives, so I earnestly hope that everything that happens from today onward will be realized according to the purpose You have planned.  
Please protect all the remaining time, Father, and I earnestly ask that You allow us to have a moment of victory. I believe that countless warriors of unification are praying for this time, so please protect them with the same grace. I earnestly ask this, and I humbly offer all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen.  
Let us establish our homeland  
<Summary of the Message> Because humanity has no homeland, there has been no true brotherhood, true family, true nation, or true world, and there have been no joyful days. All of you are people who have lost your homeland. We have gathered here today to find that homeland.  
The highest hope and purpose of conscience  
Most people today live under the burden of conscience, which reveals that they are not living good lives but rather evil ones. This land is a place where our ancestors shed tears of blood for goodness, and it is a land that should be blessed.  
Pioneering means starting anew and cultivating what has not been touched by others. Pioneering cannot be done alone. We must unite to pioneer this Earth. To unite, we must have the same content and purpose.  
The human spirit runs toward beautiful mountains and seas. The term ‘beloved hometown’ in this song refers to the place imbued with our blood, sweat, and tears. And the land we live on is the land chosen by our Father, so it is infinitely precious.  
October 7, 1964 (Wednesday), Suwon Church.  
* This message was given while explaining the lyrics of the patriotic song at the Gyeonggi region assembly and is compiled from the 12th issue of <Gyeonggi Front>. The title was added by the editor.  
The present world is extremely unstable. Countless humans are like this, and so are you. While the heart moves toward the purpose established by God, the body cannot keep up with it. What the heart and conscience work on together is universally acknowledged. Conscience commands those in dire circumstances to give more of what is theirs. The commands of conscience are endless. Even after doing good, it does not stop there but continues to appeal to the body to do even greater things.  
What is the heart? It is to command someone to sell their house and help the needy, even if they have no dinner. But what is conscience? It is to command one to give everything to the needy, embracing the heavens and the earth. Conscience even demands that God be given.  
Yet, conscience desires to place God in the best place. Moreover, conscience can only rest after seeing God giving everything to all people.  
The more one has conscience, the more they want to give the best. The most precious and good thing in the world is God. Therefore, conscience introduces God. The conscientious person wants to give even to God. The first principle of conscience is to inherit God’s hopes, circumstances, and love.  
Conscience was meant to inherit God’s hopes, circumstances, and love, but due to the fall, it has fallen to the very bottom of hell. If our ancestors had not fallen, all 3 billion of humanity would have inherited conscience, but because of the fall, it has fallen to the very bottom of hell.  
Just as water seeps out whenever there is a crack, so does conscience. Conscience endlessly calls to give. To give means to establish a connection. The giver is the subject, and the receiver is the object.  
The highest hope and purpose of conscience is to inherit the world of God’s hopes. Each individual longs to possess God in the end times. Conscience does not die until it meets God, who governs all and rules over Him. Because of this conscience, God carries out the providence of salvation.  
The purpose of conscience is to meet the protagonist who governs happiness. Without meeting Him, humanity cannot be happy. Therefore, conscience must help fulfill what He desires and wishes to accomplish. He is the owner of freedom, happiness, and ideals, and the true person.  
The true person can be said to be something greater than heaven and earth, compressed and gathered together. The time will inevitably come when the truth will explode. At that time, nothing false will remain.  
The Way is a reduction of the direct short distance of conscience. The greater the Way, the better it introduces God. The highest religion among religions is one that teaches God as Father, and the greatest of all Way Masters is one who presents the truest faith. Moreover, the true Way is to lead and properly introduce the affection of brotherhood.  
In this regard, Christianity can be considered the highest religion because it is closest to the distance of conscience and has the conditions to find them all at once.  
Where is history flowing?  
But where is history flowing? It flows to where conscience demands, that is, to where the victors of individual, family, society, nation, and even global conscience remain.  
The Messiah is the one who came to possess God, whom conscience desires, and to give that God to all humanity. However, because there were many obstacles before Him, He started from the individual and walked the path of global wandering.  
Jacob is the one who walked the path of wandering without infringing upon the world his heart desires. Thus, Israel gained the name of victory, and through victorious individuals and families, the Israelite nation was able to flourish.  
Although God wanted to be with all of Israel’s offensives, they did not move according to God’s will, so God withdrew His hand. Despite having cooperated with them, the Israelite nation killed Jesus, so God’s providence left this nation and horizontally established its foundation among the Gentiles. This is today’s Christianity.  
Humanity walks the path of a wandering traveler. In today’s world, when victorious individuals, families, and nations emerge, where is there a country to welcome them? Everywhere they go, there are enemies. Jesus came as the victor of conscience to give everything, but since the nation did not accept Him, that nation became an enemy. Thus, Christianity has walked an even more extreme path.  
The one who was to conquer Rome and establish Israel before God during His lifetime was Jesus. Had that been accomplished, Christianity would have completed a global Israel in its 2,000 years of history. It is regrettable that Israel could believe in historical great figures but could not see the Messiah who became reality.  
The Unification Church is a church of tears that believes in the sorrowful Jesus who was oppressed and could not fulfill His will. The cross is a scaffold for sinners and is something God dislikes. Was there anyone who prepared a room, a bowl of rice, or a piece of clothing to welcome the Messiah at that time?  
The fact that Jesus was born in a stable is undoubtedly a great sorrow for Him as a crown prince. If the 4,000 years of suffering of the Israelite nation was according to God’s plan, how can they be called the chosen people?  
Jesus’ hope was not to see those who believed in Him well. What God desires is not heaven. Heaven is a place to go later. God’s hope is the restoration of the universe. What must be done first is to become a loyal subject centered on God’s hope.  
“If God’s resentment remains, please pour it out on our Unification Church members. Do not let us tire or die.” This is what we should pray.  
The purpose of the Messiah’s coming 2,000 years ago was to unify the world centered on Rome and restore it before His will. Until that day comes, the Israelite nation must remain a wandering nation.  
The day when the purpose of our conscience is resolved must come quickly. That day will come when a group centered on conscience forms a nation and a state. Will God come to find a miserable place?  
The era in which science and religion are said to have no relation has passed.  
The end is coming. At the end, the goats and the sheep will be separated. The sheep know their master, while the goats do not. To say that there is no God is the greatest Satan.  
The desired nation and homeland are the destination of a wandering person. Where will we settle and establish a base? Let us raise our flags and move forward for the sake of God’s homeland and the liberation of our country. The one who says we should do this from Korea is Teacher Moon of the Unification Church.  
There is only one truth. It is where God’s heart, circumstances, and wishes align. Where might that be? It is not where denominations are, but where true people are. There are countless religions and denominations on earth, but that is not the issue. The question is who is the greatest. The one who holds the seal of God in the end times is the master.  
Heaven is wherever Jesus is welcomed, whether in a palace or a hut. Jesus, as God’s crown prince, comes to find that place adorned and fragrant, shining for eternity. Did Jesus become the Messiah after dying? Was He not the Messiah while He was alive?  
The individual representative, the family representative, the national representative wandered, and the global representative wandered. Because Jesus wandered, those who bear the mission of restoration in the end times will also wander.  
Let us establish God’s homeland.  
Let us make the land of Korea the best place in the world. Unification Church members are a wandering group. The era of national wandering is now. The place where wanderers will settle is the homeland of hope.  
Wanderers do not care about what they eat, sleep, or wear. If they do not perish and gather together, will not Jesus and God come to where they are?  
I must be able to say that I have shown such loyalty for God. How can I see the scenic spots of my country with joy when I have not even seen the scenic spots of the enemy’s country? That feeling is patriotism.  
Unification Church members must go barefoot to establish their homeland. Can we save this country with what is left over from our meals? When will we be able to focus on eating, dressing, and traveling? Let us pioneer with bare feet and bare hands. The place where such work is done is the Unification Church.  
As a man born, there are many things to do, so what need is there for many words? Unification Church members must become practical people. For the sake of the country, they must be loyal, and for the sake of the world, they must give everything. To give, one must truly give, so that the world can be saved.  
God is working to find and establish true humans. To follow the Master, who is persecuted and shedding tears, we must weep together, and to follow the Master who is starving or living in prison, we must suffer together.  
God had hoped for 4,000 years to fulfill His will in the nation of Israel but could not do so, so Jesus, from a sorrowful position, has been working hard until now, holding onto God’s grievances and frustrations, praying for forgiveness for those who do not know. God has been holding onto and guiding the Gentile nations until today. The people of the Way are scattered around the world, symbolizing the 600,000 of Israel. They are all the reserve troops of the Unification Church.  
To walk the path of faith with one’s life on the line, one must pass three tests: the test of Satan, the test of the prophets, and the test of angels. However, Unification Church members can pass through safely. Since you know all the contents of the Principle, you cannot withhold it from the people of the world. If you do not teach it, your descendants will be unhappy.  
You must know that it was Satan who killed Jesus, and it was God who brought Him back to life. You must believe and understand the deep content of Jesus’ resurrection, but today’s Christianity does not know or believe in that deep content, so it is empty.  
Let us wander until we can believe in and serve God well.  
People also want to go where they are welcomed and loved. The Lord also wants to come to where people are sincerely devoted to Him, even at the cost of death. Because Jesus walked the path of Golgotha, Christianity has developed nationally and globally based on Jesus’ victorious Golgotha. That is the history of Christianity.
Today, the Unification Church is the place to overcome the global Golgotha. Let us surely fulfill God's hope by transcending the global Golgotha.

If it is said that dedicating oneself for the nation is true, then adorning oneself for personal gain is false. The way to distinguish between truth and falsehood is to discern those who can deny themselves for a greater cause from those who cannot.

The last wandering nation that remains true on this earth is a nation that wants to give, give, and give for the world. The Unification Church members of Korea are a wandering nation seeking to find the homeland that all people desire.

Give with your heart for the sake of all humanity, and act with that intention. Until the day when we achieve our goals and fulfill our hopes in accordance with our determined objectives, do not die, do not fall, but move forward.

What kind of father is a father?

<Summary of the Message> The day of hope that God intended at the time of creation has not yet come. The sorrow of God, who looks at this fallen world, grows greater the more one wishes for that day of hope.

Since humans are the main culprits of the fall, they must naturally endure the pain and sorrow that come with it; however, God has walked the path of suffering many times over due to the sorrow humans have faced.

If humanity as a whole does not resolve this collective resentment, there can be no liberation from God. To achieve this, absolute obedience to heaven's command is necessary. However, because humans have failed to do so, God has come forth to pave the way for liberation in place of humanity. He has taken on the fight at the front lines for us.

The struggle on the path of restoration must not stop at mere victory. This victory must be connected from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, world, and heaven.

The history of 6,000 years has been about finding the lost family of Adam. Today, the world is divided into the two worlds of Cain and Abel. God desires to govern by dividing individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world into two. The Messiah came to establish the standard for unifying these two worlds.

Since humanity fell during the growth stage, two-thirds of Cain's side belongs to Satan. The outwardly manifested world consists of the Satanic world aligned with Cain and the Abel-aligned world.

The Messiah is the one who has come to restore the Abel-like individuals, families, tribes, nations, and world.

As the time for Cain's world to end has come, there must be an altar representing Cain's side to offer sacrifices; however, there cannot be only Cain's side present. Thus, an Abel-like altar must emerge.

From Abel's perspective, the group that has arisen to connect the altar from today to tomorrow, from this month to next month, and from this year to next year is the group of unification. Therefore, we must manage the Cain-like world and the Abel-like world and connect them to heaven's side.

God is seeking one nation. Jesus sought to govern the Israelite nation. If the Israelite nation had accepted Jesus, He would have realized God's ideals on this earth as a living sacrifice.

The Messiah must achieve victory personally, as well as at the family, national, and global levels. If Jesus had achieved personal victory, Satan would not have been able to invade that individual, and if he had proclaimed victory at the family level, Satan would not have been able to invade that family. If Jesus had established a victorious Israelite nation, he would not have died. The reason Jesus was rejected by the Israelite nation was that there was no Cain-like altar where he could stand.

Following the history of the treacherous Israelite nation leads to Christianity's fate of becoming a wandering customer like them.

Abel must manage the offerings of Cain, and the offerings that Abel manages are received by God. An Abel who can subdue Cain must come again. Since there is a Cain-like altar but no Abel-like altar yet, He must come again to build this altar.

A representative of Cain who can globally manage the mistakes of Cain's offerings must come.

The time has come to cry out for the resurrection of Abel-like individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world. God is calling Abel who has triumphed over Cain.

Those who enjoy glory and fame as individuals in this world will perish. That glory and fame do not belong to individuals but to heaven; if they are not returned to heaven, they will perish.

History calls for the resurrection of the body of Abel's victory, that is, the resurrection of individual, family, tribe, nation, and world victory. That person is the Messiah.

The Lord who is coming is the great king of historical sorrow and the judge of justice. He comes to judge the unjust and defend the good.

God is calling Abel who can judge Cain. This is to judge Cain, forgive sins, and liberate him.

Even if this teacher here dies, the will he sought must remain. Even if we die, this will must remain.

In fulfilling the will, even if thirty million are sacrificed, God will not mind greatly.

You and I are enemies. However, centered around ideology, we are comrades.

Every time you go to bed, you should be immersed in the conviction that this hand connects with thirty million and with three billion humanity. In such a place, there is God's hope.

Let us explode ourselves. Let us build a tower higher than Mount Everest in the Himalayas. We must not remain silent. If it is to relieve God's resentment, let us accomplish anything in an instant.

Today, both the democratic world and the communist world are leaning. God is seeking Abel who can redeem Cain.

Today, our Unification Church must transcend the idea of a chosen people and adopt the idea of a common people. The chosen people are those nations that Satan can invade, while the common people are those nations that can win in the fight against Satan and establish the sovereignty of the Messiah. Furthermore, the chosen people are nations where Satan's sovereignty remains, while the common people are nations that can subdue Satan and redeem Cain.

God is demanding that we repay the historical enemies. God seeks to plant roots in the Korean Peninsula to resolve the historical resentment of 6,000 years and to navigate the great sea. We must be in a conviction that leads thirty million people and ties them to me, challenging the vast sea, saying, "Storm, blow! Let’s see who wins, you or me."

Blessed families must not only be parents of their families but also become parents of at least their tribes and nations. If you do not have the conviction to love your nation, you will receive wrath. Jesus embraced heaven and earth with His ideology.

Goodness is to forget oneself and seek to establish something greater. If one forgets society and loves their own family, they will be judged by society. Likewise, if a leader loves their family more than their nation, they will be judged by the nation. Those in charge must understand that they must fight against sin.

The teacher may leave this country soon. When the teacher went to Japan in the past, he cried out, "My homeland, beloved thirty million people, I will go and return," carrying the resentment of liberation.

I have never loved the parents who gave birth to me. To pass on the historical legacy to you, you must endure hardships.

The age of restoration is said to be the age of saints. However, if we trust and leave everything to those who are silent, heaven will perish, and that cannot be allowed. Even if we are asleep, the will is gradually approaching us. The time has come; we must work hard.

As we look forward to the seven-year milestone beyond forty years, no matter how we think about it, the will is absolute. God does not call people to eat bread on the day of the feast but calls workers, those who can manage the feast.

When it gets cold, all the leaves fall. Let the Unification Church become the branches of the tree. The established churches are the leaves that will fall after being hit by frost.

God is calling those who will take responsibility for the earth; we must choose to be either the seekers or the offerings.

At this time, the last of the 6,000-year struggle, God is looking for people like Joshua and Caleb.

How have you been before the Father? What will you do? You must belong to one of these. We must go forth believing in heaven from the position of responsibility. What will you do for the one who is to come, and what will you leave for your descendants? If there is nothing, you will receive historical judgment.

God is a pitiful being. He has labored for 6,000 years to find loyal subjects. Today's Unification Church is pitiful. If this pity ends in pity, then God does not exist. However, we are not pitiful because God exists.

We must embrace this nation and this world and comfort God. We must not call the advancing Father from behind but must say before the Father, "Father, the front I am responsible for is without issue. Please rest assured." When the Father follows me, bearing the historical responsibility, and is comforted, heaven will become mine. Such a person is a filial son of heaven. The teacher wants to make you such a person. Before the nation suffers, let us suffer first. Let us harmonize and unify.

The conclusion is this: What position will you serve God from? The Father must be able to follow me and shed tears.

Our life is but a moment. Even if we live for a hundred years, it is only 36,500 days. During that time, let us be those who repay before the foundation of heart left by God.

<Original Loyalty, Filial Piety, and Passion>

<Summary of the Message> Blessed families must break free from their past notions of life. Originally, the ideal couple created by God should give glory to God, but due to the fall, they returned sorrow instead of glory. This involves not only the responsibility of Adam and Eve but also the unfaithfulness of the archangel. The angel should have established the way of loyalty and filial piety to God first, but he fell without doing so. Therefore, the providence of restoration is to establish loyalty, filial piety, and passion.

However, no matter how much we strive for loyalty, filial piety, and passion, we cannot reach the original standard. This is because it is loyalty, filial piety, and passion from the standpoint of the enemy. We tend to speak and think of loyalty, filial piety, and passion conventionally, but original loyalty, filial piety, and passion are not like that. Therefore, a central point is needed.

Since God has established the mental center of loyalty, filial piety, and passion, all religions and paths must come to establish this. All practitioners have come to find and establish this, and Jesus also came to find a family to establish loyalty and filial piety. God established the Israelite nation to find such a family. Jesus should have first established the way of loyalty and filial piety and become a priest to establish it to subdue Satan.

Originally, children, when they mature, should represent God's ideals and reality. Blessed families must not be outdone by anyone in establishing loyalty, filial piety, and passion. Loyalty, filial piety, and passion must start from the family. Blessing is inheriting the Father's hope. Until now, there has been loyalty and filial piety towards God, but there has been no passion in the family. Before the day of God comes, passion cannot be established, and as long as Satan's accusations remain, passion cannot be established.

Those present here must not be accused. You must become those who can be recognized by heaven and earth and by Satan.

You who are blessed by God must fulfill your responsibilities as parents. You must lead your family emotionally, practically, and economically. There will come a time when what you have not done in this country will become a grievance. If you cannot fulfill your responsibilities, you will be expelled from this country. Couples must work for their nation and the world. If you endure hardships, everything will connect.

From next year, it is time to work for the world for three years. The path of restoration is not for one's own benefit. It is for the sake of others and those who follow. The teacher must pass through three countries, and at that time, you must be able to dance to the teacher's tune.

When the teacher goes abroad with the mother, the connection with this country will be severed. That is why he leaves the mother behind. It is like Jesus leaving the Holy Spirit behind. If the teacher longs for Korea, he must leave the baby and the mother behind.

God governs through three stages: the Word, all things, and reality. The Word is the greatest asset. Blessing is also precious. Be a person who acts according to the Word. Give and give again. And love the one who gave the Word. Always carry any burden. And have the thought of wanting to harmonize. You must have a lot of interest in the teacher.

Judgment is done by the law of love. To become loyal subjects, you must strike down the traitors and make things smooth, and to become filial children, you must repay your parents' enemies. You must not think of anything outside of the will.

Those who give must prepare more than those who receive. No one can handle the most precious thing according to their own will.

Love the ideology more than anything else.

Blessed families should endure hardships, but do not show the light of those hardships on your faces. Endure hardships without others knowing.

You are now in the completion stage of the growth period. You must become the completion stage of the completion period to stand at a global standard.

Since there remains a path to embrace the opposing nation, the teacher embraces the wrong family members. If he were to abandon them, it would result in the sacrifice of the entire nation, so even if they make mistakes while working, he forgives them.

A family is a sanctuary, and the belongings of that family are sacrificial vessels, and the head of the family is the representative of the Word.

<The Suffering of Jesus on the Cross>

<Prayer> We know that the Father's wish will surely be fulfilled on this earth, and the wishes of the good ancestors will also surely be fulfilled on this earth.

We believe that there will come a time when the Father's wish and our wish will be fulfilled in one place, and a true child who can give glory to the Father will appear in this universe. We know that our ancestors also went through the path of death, the path of tears, and the path of blood, longing for that grace.

Today, the place we must go is not a place to fulfill our own wishes, nor a place to seek our own joy, nor a place where this reality can be joyful and glorious, nor a place where numerous nations wish for their own prosperity and glory. No matter how rugged, sorrowful, lonely, painful, or confronted with the path of death, we wish to go toward the place where the Father desires, the place our ancestors longed for while dying for the will of goodness. Going to that place is the wish of the individual, the wish of the family, the wish of this nation and this world, and we ask that you allow us to realize once again that this is the destination for all humanity in the future.

We earnestly wait for the day of victory when we can meet the Father at that place and inherit the entire legacy of our ancestors. Along with this, we hope to sing the glory of the Father and fulfill our own resolution, becoming the true sons and daughters of the Father who can boast of the glory of victory for eternity.

We ask that you find such children and that the day when you can receive the glory you long for through that place must come quickly to this earth. We know that you have been governing until today by connecting numerous altars of blood to fulfill that day for humanity.

When we look at this world today, what can bring joy to the Father? What will be the foundation of such a center? Humanity must think about this.
unable to do so. Moreover, this country and this nation, which should be responsible for and lead all historical issues, are also unaware. 

In the midst of others' ignorance, we must seek the path to establish the intentions that our Father has held, while worrying about the efforts He has made. We must recognize how sad, how wronged, and how unjust it is that we are connected through the places where our Father has been oppressed, chased, struggled, bled, and shed tears. We earnestly hope and wish for permission to realize this once again. 

Countless humans are seeking their own happiness, and many nations are only hoping for their own national interests. However, all of this does not come to fruition as our Father intended; rather, it adds sorrow and resentment to our Father and violates His heart. We earnestly hope and wish that our Father will have compassion on all these nations and peoples who do not know.

May the day of joy when we can do so come quickly. We are struggling for that day, so Father, please do not worry. We earnestly hope and wish to be children who can do what is possible. 

We are walking a path that others do not know. This path is the one our Father walks, so we have stepped forward, leaving behind all things in the world. 

Reflecting on the past, there have been many paths of suffering and paths of tears. Our Father knows the fact that we have wandered through the rough stony paths and thorny paths. All of this was for our Father, to find a day of glory for Him, to testify with Him, and to establish the standard of glory on earth. Our Father knows this. 

Those who have come out along this path to seek our Father should have become a multitude praising Him in glory, yet many have come and gone without doing so. Here, these people are also weary. There is still much work left to be done. Nevertheless, our Father is still seeking the true form that can give new glory to Him in this one place. We earnestly hope and wish that our Father, who has come to us with a historically sad heart that must not be neglected, will accept us.

We have nothing to show before Him without shame, and we have nothing to comfort Him with. I know that there is no one who is shedding tears for this country and this nation, who is willing to do anything for the new history of this nation.
